"vaṁdē kuvalayabhūsaṇamaiṇunasāōdayaṁ visālacchaṁ । tribhaimarahiyaṁ māṇasasaraṁ va paḍhamaṁ jiṇaṁ paḍhamaṁ ॥ 1 ॥
vimavaṇasōṇayalaṁ phuraṁtakari-mayara mīṇa-saṁkhaṁkaṁ । paṇamāmi sāyaraṁ sāyaraṁ va vīrassa kamakamalaṁ ॥ 2 ॥
haiyamōhaghaṇatamōhā nimmalamōhā virāipaumōhā । sēsā vi hutu jaiṇō jiṇavaṅgō divasavaṇō vva ॥ 3 ॥
sitrapayasaravarahaṁ sē pahīṇanīsēsa punna-pāvasē । kēvalakaraniyariddhē paṇamaha siddhē susamiddhē ॥ 4 ॥

kalāvaībhāya jayasēgakumārassa araṇṇē dattēṇa saha saṁbaṁdhō ।
phurai puṇa majjha hiyaai 'ajjhā dēvassa cētra uciya tti । niyasāmiyaṁ pamōttuṁ rayaṇaṁ kō maihara annassa ? ॥69॥
kulagirisamunbhavāṇaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ rayaṇāyarō hu sariyāṇaṁ । mōtcūna chudaihīraṁ gadaṁtarē ghaḍai kiṁ juṇhā ?' ॥ 70 ॥
ēvaṁ vibhāviūṇaṁ appaḍitrāē tīē paḍivaṁ । dēvasta daṁsiyaṁ mēṁ, saṁpai dēvō pamāṇaṁ ti" ॥ 71 ॥
ēvaṁ dattēṇa bhaṇiē mayaṇasaradhōraṇīvihuriyaṁ cittaphalagāvalōyaṇa vāulattēṇā'thaikamukahuṁkāraṁ va rāyāṇamuvalabbha
bhaṇiyaṁ dhīdhaṇamaṁtiṇā 'bhō sēṭṭhiputta ! suṁdaraṁ taē bhaṇiyaṁ, jaō-
ēsā dhōyakalaṁkapactraṇa nisānāhōtramāṇāṇaṇā, papphulluppalalōlalōyaṇajuyā lāyannanīrappavā ।
dēvaṁ dēvasamāṇarūvavihavaṁ mōttūṇa kassōciyā ?, jāṇaṁtō rayaṇāvaliṁ kuṇai kō kāyassa kaṁṭhē buhō ?' ॥72॥
taō bhaṇiyaṁ maisārēṇa rāyamittēṇa -
'ajjhā hāvirahārihārasariyā rāyanniyaṁvatthalā, nēttaṁbhōyavirāiyāsasarasī vacchōyatuṁgāyalā ।

5 yānivahanahī paḍhamāṇapabhūyabhaṭṭa - caṭṭō divasasēsaṁ syaṇiṁ cāivāhiūṇa duiyadiyahē pahāṇamaṁti-sāmaṁtaparivuḍō sayala-

1
ētthaṁtarē varaṁgō kumāramaṁtī lasaṁtamuhakaṁtī । bhaṇai 'pahu ! amha pahuṇō hariyaṁ hiyayaṁ tuha guṇēhiṁ ॥ 106 ॥
taha kaha visarūvaṁ vō siddhaṁ dattēṇa vaṇiyaputtēga । jaha ṭaṁkukkinaṁ pitra ṭhiyamayalaṁ cittabhittī ॥ 107 ॥
tā tēṇa tumha ēyaṁ saṁdiṭṭhē nēhanibbharaṁ dhīra ! । tuha guṇanihiṇō dūraṭṭiyā hu kaṁ gauratraṁ kuṇimō ? || 108 ॥
kā tassa chēyayā ?, kā udārayā ?, kō guṇēsu aṇurāō ? । viyarai jō na guṇīṇaṁ pasatyavatthaṁ suiddhaṁ pi ॥ 109
tā guruguṇāṇurāyā lāyamnakalākalāvaguṇakaliyā । aivallahā vi bālā ēsā saṁpēsiyā tumha ॥ 110॥
na ya ēyāē rāō jāō annēsu rāyakumarēsu । kamalāyaraṁ pamōttuṁ kattha va kamalā raī kuṇau ॥ 111 ॥
tā ēyāē pārṇi paṇaīyaṇapaṇayapālaṇappavaṇa ! । giṇhējja tumaṁ supurisa !, karēsu maṇanivvuī amha ॥ 112 ॥
na kayāi diṭṭhēnisurya ēīē vippiyaṁ mamāō vi । tā taha karējja jaha mē na sarai kariṇi vtra vijjhassa ॥113॥
kiṁ vā kuluggayāṇaṁ puraō parijapiēṇa bahuēṇa ? । paḍivanavacchalā tē sahāvaō cēva jaṁ huṁti' ।। 114 ॥
upphālikaṇa ēvaṁ viraē maṁtimmi niuṇabhaṇiyammi । paḍibhaṇai rāyasaṁkhō saṁkhō iva mahuranigghōsō ॥ 115 ॥
“avtrō ! kiṁ pi auvvaṁ sōjanaṁ vijayanaravariṁdassa । amhāṇaṁ pi guṇēhiṁ raṁjijjai jēṇa sē hiyayaṁ ॥ 116॥
jai bālayā vi amhē jaṇayaviōgēṇa nitrapayaṁ pattā । kiṁ tēttiēṇa guṇiṇō jāyā uttāgamaiṇō vi ? | 117॥
ghaṇaguṇarasapunnāī purisaphalāī havaṁti pariṇāmē । taruṇāī nigguṇāiṁ sauṇāṇa maṇaṁ na raṁjaṁti ॥ 118 ॥
ahavā-
dōsē vi guṇē cciya parajaṇassa pēcchaṁti uttamā lōyā । chāyāharaṁ pi na muyai himakiraṇō laṁchaṇaṁ jēṇa ॥ 119॥
tahā-
jāṇaṁti piyam̐ ciyavōttumuttamā amayamuttiṇō nūṇaṁ । kiṁ amayāō anaṁ jhariuṁ mayalaṁchaṇō muṇai ? ॥ 120 ॥
tā tassa puipahuṇō nikāraṇavacchalassa guṇanihiṇō। kaha na karissāmi ahaṁ vayaṇaṁ naṇu jaṇayatullassa ? " ॥ 121
aha jayasēṇakumārō pabhaṇai dattaṁ sabhāgayaṁ hasirō । “ajja'mha tumha vayaṇē savisēsaṁ paccaō jāō ॥ 122 ॥
jaō-
ērisamaśuddhayattaṁ, ēsō nayasuṁdarī vayaṇavihavō । dakkhina - viṇaya uciyannuyāō dēvē auvvāō ॥ 123 ॥
taha vi na tōsō niyaguṇagaṇēṇa paraguṇasuīsu aṇurāō | ahavā ērisaya cciya mahāṇubhāvā, jaō bhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 124 ॥
bhariyabhruvaṇaṁtarēhiṁ viguṇēhiṁ niyaēhiṁ kuṁdadhavalēhiṁ । taha tūsaṁti na dhīrā jaha paraguṇalēsasavaṇēṇa ॥ 125 ॥

ṇayaṁ" ti । ēyaṁ rāyatrayaṇamatakkiyacaḍēṁ kānitrāyadāruṇamāyaniūṇa sayalapariyaṇō aṇṇōṣṇavayaṇāvayacchaṇaviṇi-
cchiyacchiyalō 'hā ! kimēyaṁ ?' ti kayatriyappō sunnavunnō khaṇamacchiya samakālamukkalallukapōkkō vilaviuṁ payattō-
'hā ajjautta ! anagghiṇō si, kaha vavasiyaṁ taē ēyaṁ ? । sā muhamaṁḍaṇamamhaṁ kattha ? 'ti bhaṇati jāyāō ॥201॥
'hā ! rāyaṁgaṇamēyaṁ vaṭṭa sunnaṁ va taṁtriṇā suddhaṁ । mā rūsa, pasiya āṇēmu sāmi ! taṁ' pariyaṇō bhaṇai ॥ 202॥
' hā hatti kiṁ kimēyaṁ ?, ghī ghī ēyārisaṁ vihivihāṇaṁ' । nara-nārigaṇō nayarē ruyai samaṁtā iya bhaṇatō ॥ 203 ॥
darabhuttayaṁ pi bhattaṁ darapīyaṁ pāṇiyaṁ pi paricattaṁ । ḍiṁbhēhiṁ vi tammi diṇē mukkaṁ thanaṁ pi kimu annaṁ ? ॥ 204 ॥
akaṁdasaddabhīmaṁ nikaruṇāṇaṁ pi jaṇiyakārunnaṁ । daṭṭhūṇa puraṁ rāyā ussuyacittō puṇō āha ।। 205 ।।
'bhō maṁti ! kiṁ cirāvaha ? kiṁ na yaṇaha majjha vēyaṇaṁ aṁgē ? | hā ! niṭhuraṁ na phuhai hiyayaṁ mē garuyadukkhaṁ pi' ॥ 206॥
aha maṁti-dāra-sayaṇā saiṁyarāhamudāharati rūyamāṇā । " mā kuṇa viyakkhaṇa ! khaē khārakkhēvaṁ khaṇēsa mha ॥ 207॥
jai kaha vi buddhikhūṇaṁ saṁjāyaṁ dēvvajōgaō ēgaṁ । tā mā karēha vīyaṁ gaṁḍōvari phōḍiyātulaṁ ॥ 208 ॥
bhayakāyarāṇa saraṇaṁ havaṁti dhīrā dharāharatthējjā । dhīrā vi dhīrayaṁ jaṛa cayaṁti tā hōu kiṁ saraṇaṁ ? ॥ 209 ॥
annaṁ ca-
cira parivāliyamēyaṁ rajjamasaṁpattasattusaṁtātraṁ । hayavippahayaṁ hōhī tumaē mukaṁ muhuttēṇa ॥ 210 ॥
kāūṇa kulacchēyaṁ mā pūra maṇōrahē rivujaṇassa । pajjāliūṇa bhavaṇaṁ kō ujjōyaṁ kuṇai maimaṁ ?" ।। 211 ॥
iya saviṣayaṁ sapaṇayaṁ guṇa-dōsaviyārasāramavi bhaṇiyaṁ । avaganiūṇa rāyā caliō aṇutāvatattaṁgō ॥ 212 ॥
na tahā tavēi tavaṇō na jaliyajalagō na vijjunigdhāō । jaha aviyāriyakajjaṁ visaṁvayaṁtaṁ tatrai jaṁtuṁ ॥ 213||
tattō aṇugammaṁtō samaṁti- muddhaṁta - patti - paurēhiṁ । kaha kaha vi aṇicchaṁtō vi turayamārōviō tēhiṁ ॥ 214 ॥

rūvāisayaviṇijjiyasuraṁgaṇā saha sahīhiṁ kīlaṁtī । pañcakrakhā iva kamalā kamalā nāmēṇa savilāsā ॥ 227 ॥ 10

luddhō ghaṇēṇa, ramaṇīhiṁ kāmuō, patthivō tri puhavīē । viusō subhāsiēhiṁ kō saṁpattō jaē tittiṁ 1 ॥ 229 ॥
kōhalāirēgā ubvūḍhā maggiūṇa sā tēṇa । annannavāulassa ya pamhuṭṭhā sā puṇō tassa ॥ 230 ॥
cirakālā puṇaravi tahēva saṁpattapōḍhimā diṭṭhā | aṇurāyavasā puṭṭhō niyamittō ' kā ṇu ēsa ?' tti ॥231॥
siddhaṁ ca tēṇa hasiuṁ 'naṇu ēsā tumha cēva dēvi ' tti । jā mamgiūṇa tajhyā vitrāhiyā baḍakōḍḍēṇa ॥ 232 ॥ 15
ri ṁ cirassa rāyā ciṁtaṛa aṇutāvanibbharō tāhē । 'hā ! kaha maē varāī pavaṁciyā mūḍhacittēṇa ? ॥ 233 ॥
tārunnē mahavēṇāō kassa va maṇaṁ na pīḍaṁti ? | aisutthi ēṇa muraṁ sahāviyā tā maē ēsā ' ॥ 234 ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ ca 'mitta ! kiṁ puṇa pautthavaiya va saṁtanēvacchā। maṁgalavalayāharaṇā dīsai paridubbalaṁgī ya ? ॥ 235 ॥

iyarēhiṁ puṇō vr̥ttaṁ 'nivvinnā mō vivāyavāyāō । tā tāya ! kayapasāyaṁ chiṁdasu vavahāramamhāṇaṁ' ॥ 304 ॥
āha taō pasuvālō “puttā ! sō tumha saṁtiō tāō । āsi aipaṁḍiō naṇu ēgaṁtahiō ya tumhāṇaṁ ॥ 305 ॥
jaṁ jassa hiyaṁ jaṁ jassa dhāriṇaṁ pariṇaīē suhaphalayaṁ । taṁ tassa tēṇa diṣnaṁ ucaēsapahāṇamēyaṁ tu ।। 306॥
jassa kalasamma rēṇū dināī tassa tēṇa chēttāī । 'kisikammaṁ ciya phalayaṁ tuha' ti ēsō ya uvaēsō ॥307॥
aṭṭhīṇi ditaēṇa dinnaṁ gō-mahisi turaya-karahāī । taha ēyapōsaṇaṁ ciya uvaihaṁ suṭhu suhajaṇayaṁ ॥ 308 ॥
vahiyādāṇēṇa puṇō siddhaṁ taṁ rāyalēhaō hōjja । ahatrā vi haṭṭavaṇiō ginhējja dhaṇaṁ dhurāhiṁtō ॥ 309 ॥
ēsa puṇa savvalahuā kisikammāīṇa vāḍhamasamatthō । gahiyadīṇāradavyō kalaṁtarājīvaō hōjjā ॥ 310. ॥

tubhē sikkhiyā kira lakkhissaha ēttiyaṁ sayaṁ cētra । iya jaṇaēṇa vi mannē visēsaō kiṁ pi nō bhaṇiyā ||312॥
tā tucchadhaṇassa kaē mā nimnēhā parōpparaṁ hōha | saṁbharaha jaṇayabhaṇiyaṁ, sahōyarā dulahā lōē ||313|| avi ya-
ailāliyā vi aipāliyā vi vihaḍaṁti sēsayā sayaṇā । huṁti sahējjā trihurē kutriyā tri sahōyarā cēva" ॥314॥
iya thēramaṁtiyaṁ payaḍajuttiyaṁ suṇiya muṇiyatattēhiṁ । bāhajalōlliyalōyaṇajuēhiṁ savvēhiṁ sahasa tti ।। 315 ॥
āliṁgiūṇa bhaṇiō sōmō 'vacchaya ! anāyatattēhiṁ । saṁtātriō si suiraṁ taṁ khamiyanvaṁ tara savvaṁ ।। 316 ॥
iyarēṇa vipattiṁ ' maē tri annāṇa- lōhamūḍhēṇa । jaṁ atriṇaēṇa bhaṇiyā marisējjada saṁpayaṁ taṁ pi' ॥ 317 ॥
pasuvāla va pattō savvēhiṁ vi 'amha tāyacattāṇaṁ । karuṇārasiēṇa taē suṭṭha kayaṁ ajja tāyattaṁ ' ॥ 318 ॥
iya kayabahusaṁbhāsaṁ hijjō gēhāgaēhiṁ tuḍēhiṁ । purajaṇajaṇiyāṇaṁdaṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ kayaṁ tēhiṁ ॥ 319 ॥
tā ēttha imaṁ cōjaṁ aṭṭhinayarēṇa muktvayērēṇa । iya giuganīisāraṁ vatrahārō ērisō chinnō || 320 ॥
[ dhaṇasēṭṭhiputta cakka vivāyachēyagapa suvālakkhā ṇayaṁ samattaṁ. 1

aha sanbhēhiṁ sa bhaṇiō 'sacca saca, mahaṁtamacchariyaṁ । aivisamō vabahārō kaha chinnō gāmagōhēṇa ?" ॥321 ॥
āyaniūṇa ēyaṁ rāyā maulaṁtavayaṇasarasiruhō । hiyayakhuḍukkiyadukkhō triyappiuṁ ēyamāḍhattō ॥ 322 ॥
" jai tā nirakkharassa vi gāmēllapasussa ērisaṁ nāṇaṁ ।, satthatthakōviyāē tā tīē kiṁ na saṁbhavai ? ॥ 323 ॥
satyē vibhaṇiyamēyaṁ 'suraē pāganbhamannayā lajjā । chajjai varaṁgaṇāṇaṁ' kiṁ na muṇai sā phuḍaṁ viusī ? ॥ 324 ॥
tā savvā aṇajjō nillajjō kugasaṁgamē sajjō । nivbhaggō bhaggō haṁ tārisarayaṇassa ya ajōggō” ॥ 325॥
suiraṁ hiyaē pairicitiūṇa dīṇāṇaṇō bhagai maṁtiṁ । 'bhō maṁti ! kayaṁ pātraṁ maē mahaṁtaṁ aunēṇa ॥ 326 ॥
acchaṁtī jaṇayagharē sā varaī vihuyacitasaṁtāvā । hā ! kaha maē aṇatthaṁ nikkāraṇavēriṇā gamiyā || 327 ॥
tā savvā na sattō pāṇē dāṇiṁ muhuttamavi dhariuṁ । pauṇīkarēhi jalaṇaṁ jēṇa visōhēmi appāṇaṁ' ॥ 328 ॥
iya kayanicchayamaccaṁ tadukkhiyaṁ lakkhiūṇa taṁ maṁtī । kāūṇa rahaṁ pabhaṇai 'sāmi ! nisāmēhi paramatthaṁ ॥ 329॥
after a free hiyā 'hiyaṁ sāmiṇō na jō muṇai । suparicchiyaṁ khu kajjaṁ pariṇāmasuhāvahaṁ hōi ॥ 330 ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ ca-
paḍhamaṁ ciya rōsabharē jā buddhī hōi sā na kāyantrā । aha kīrai tā nūṇaṁ na suṁdarī tīē pariṇāmō ॥ 339॥

। 1.382-

pēcchāiyāō hacchaṁ racchāō dīhalōlanēttāhiṁ । payaḍujjalarayaṇāhiṁ ya ramaṇīhiṁ va haṭṭasōhāhiṁ ॥ 438 ॥
daramaṁḍiyagaṁḍa-daraṁjiyacchi-daraparihiyaṁbaradharāhiṁ । darabaddha cihnara-darapīyapāṇa-daranaddhahārāhiṁ ॥ 439 ||
avahatthiyarōirabālayāhiṁ avagaṇiyaguruyaṇabhayāhiṁ । paiḍahacchā hacchaṁ ciya bahūhiṁ ghara - dēulaṭṭālā ॥ 440 ॥
dēvīdaṁsaṇa kōuyamiliyāṇimisacchiramaṇiruddhāsaṁ । jāyaṁ sahasā nayaraṁ visaṭṭakamalāyarāyāraṁ ॥ 441 ॥
kāō va satōsāō siyakusumaṁjalijalēṇa dēvīē । ayasamalaṁ pitra dhōyaṁti sīlaguṇasaṁthuiparāō || 442 ॥
jaya jaya naṁda mahāsai ! jīva ciraṁ jīviēṇa amhaṁ pi । sirakayakaraṁjalīō dhuṇaṁti kāō vi tuṭṭāō ॥ 443 ॥
iya naiyarajaṇānaṁda jayaṁtīē samaṁ piyayamāē । kayamaṁgalasayalakkhaṁ rāyā niyamaṁdiraṁ pattō ॥ 444 ॥
āiṭuṁ ca visiddhaṁ dvāvaṇayaṁ nariṁdacaṁdēṇa । upphāliyasuya jammaṁ cārayaparimōyaṇāīyaṁ ॥ 445 ॥
maraṇā nitrō niyattō, miliyā dēvī, suō ya paḍhamōti । amayamayaṁ pitra bhuvaṇaṁ jaṇāṇa jāyaṁ diṇē tammi ॥ 446
taō-
dijjatadēyaṁ pijjaṁtapēyaṁ khajjatakhajjaṁ bhōjjatabhōjaṁ । vajaṁtatraj kīraṁtakajjaṁ nacatanahaṁ ghōsaṁtabhaṭṭaṁ ॥ 447 ॥
uddāmasaddaṁ bhagnantabhaddaṁ sāraṁgabhōyaṁ turaṁtalōyaṁ । maṁgalasāraṁ taṁbōlaphāraṁ tuṭṭaṁtahāraṁ rējjatadāraṁ ॥। 448 ।।
kayasayalajaṇacchēraṁ uvahasiyakubēra riddhisuṁdēraṁ । dināvāriyasattaṁ baddhāvaṇayaṁ iya pavattaṁ ॥ 449 ॥
kiṁca-
katthai nacanti naḍā, katthai kayacōjjakhujjavāmaṇayā । katthai vārabahūō, katthai kulabāliyālīō ॥ 450 ॥
dēvaula-gharaṁgaṇa-tiya- caukka - siṁghāḍa-caccarāīsu । pēcchaṇayā'māyajaṇaṁ maiḍahaṁ va puraṁ tayā jāyaṁ ॥ 451 ॥
rāsēhiṁ caccarīhiṁ ghōraṇaghōsēṇa tāragī ēhiṁ । akkhittēhiṁ surēhiṁ vi kusumēhiṁ pavarisiyaṁ tattha ।। 452 ॥
ēvaṁ pamōyasāraṁ samaikaṁtē duvālasāhammi । suhi-sayaṇa baṁdhavēhiṁ bālassa paiṭṭiyaṁ nāmaṁ || 453 ॥
jaṁ ēsa punaprattō jaṇaṇī-jaṇayāṇa jīvaṇaguṇēṇa । kalasasumiṇēṇa laddhō tā bhannau punnakalasō tti ॥ 454 ॥
ēvaṁ suhēṇa kālē vaccatē rāiṇō sabhajjassa । dēva - guru-bhattisāraṁ dhammasvaṇaṁ kuṇaṁtassa ।। 455 ॥
jāō visayavirāō ubhayāṇumaēṇa tā duvēhiṁ pi । paḍinaṁ baṁbhavayaṁ jāvajjīvaṁ gurusamīvē ॥ 456 ॥

1
taō ' ēvaṁ dēva - gurupāyāṇubhāvēṇaṁ' ti bahumanniūṇa rāyavayaṇaṁ gandhaṁ parivālayaṁtīē pāunbhūō dēvīē dēva-

kusalāṇubaṁdhikammōdaēṇa aha tassa bhōyaṇāvasarē । pattō tilōyanāhō bhikkhaṭṭhā gihaduvāram ॥ 130 ॥
taṁ pēcchiūṇa baṁdī āṇaṁdarasu mā yasavvaṁgō । paḍilāi jiṇidaṁ parivēsiya kāmaguṇi ॥ 131 ॥
ciṁtai ya 'ahaṁ dhana sahalaṁ mē jamma jīviyaṁ ajja । jaṁ bhayavaṁ dāṇamiṇaṁ paḍicchaē pāṇipuḍaēṇa' ॥ 132 ॥
ētthaṁtarammi gayaṇē ucchaliō dēvaduṁduhinināō । ghōsiṁti 'ahō dāṇaṁ ! ahō mahādāna' miha vibuhā ॥133॥
jaṇaṇiyamahacchēraṁ gaṁdhōdaya- pupphavarisaṇaṁ jāyaṁ । ukkōsā vasuhārā paḍiyā ya gharaṁgaṇē sahasā ॥ 134 ॥
avi ya-
nara-naravai - asura - surā baṁdittaṁ baṁdiṇō vi sē pattā । kiṁ vā supattadāṇā jāyai accabbhuyaṁ na jaē ? ॥ 135 ॥
iya payaḍaṁ māhappaṁ pēcchaṁtō suddhadāṇadhammassa । bhētūna kammagaṁṭhiṁ daṁsaṇasaḍḍhō imō jāō ॥ 136 ॥
viṇiōiūṇa vittaṁ pavittapattē dūriyadurāsō । caiūṇa pūidēhaṁ pattō paḍhamaṁ amaragēhaṁ ॥ 137 ॥
bhōttaṇa ciraṁ bhōē surasuṁdarivisaravāḍḍhayāmōē | caviumamarālayāō ēsō viṇadharō jāō ॥ 138 ॥
jāō jahatthanāmō imēṇa jāēṇē rayagasāribbhō । jaṇaṇī vi hu punnajasā punnajasā cētra saṁpannā ।। 139 ।।
rūvaṁ kalākalāvō lacchī kittī kalaṁkanimmukkā । aṁtēuraṁ sutāraṁ savvaṁ dāṇassa phalamēyaṁ ॥ 140 ॥

viusāṇa kulīṇāṇaṁ dhaṇīṇa dhammīṇa tadiyarāṇaṁ ca । pāyaṁ tulaguṇāṇaṁ jāyai jītrāṇa mittattaṁ ॥ 151 ॥
nēhaniraṁtarayāē tāō caurō vi pāyamēgattha । bhuṁjaṁti suvaṁti ramaṁti lōyalōyaṇakayāṁ ।। 152 ।।
kiṁ bahuṇā ?
'ēsā kajjavasēṇa vammahapiyā jāyā cauddhā ṇu kiṁ ?, dēvī kiṁ va sarassaī phuḍamahō ! ēvaṁsarūvā ṭhiyā ?' |
rūvaṁ nāṇaguṇaṁ caṇannasarisaṁ tāsiṁ samaṁ pēcchirō, jāō vimhiyamāṇasō purajaṇō ēvaṁviyappāulō ॥153॥
aha riddhisuṁdarī maṁdiraṁtiē tāhiṁ raṁmaṁtīhiṁ । nijjhāiyā kayāī pavittiṇī guṇasirī nāma ।। 154 ॥
jā kalaṁkamukkā dūriyadō suggamā thirasahāvā । niccamakhaṁḍāyārā auccagahanāhamutti ।। 155 ।।
vāsōuvva sumēhā adidōsāyarā asyasaṁgā । sasiyaradhavalaṁbarasacchamāṇasā sarayalacchi vva ।। 156 ।।
aṁgīkayaparamahimā viuḍiyakamalāyarā himōu vtra । jhijjaṁtasayaladōsā susīyalā sisiramaiya vtra ।। 157 ।।
parahuyamahurālāvāṇaṁdiyalōyā vasaṁtamutti vva । gimhamayā itra kayajaṇabaihusēyā uggatavaṇāhā ।। 158 ।।
iya saccakālasīlaṁ pavittacittaṁ pavattiṇi daṭhṭhē | bhaṇiyaṁ rāyasuyāē viyasaṁtamuhāraviṁdāē । 159 ।।
'caṁdakala va satārā kiṁkiyavēsā halā hu kā ēsā । sahiyā samāṇavēsāhiṁ rāyahaṁsi v haṁsīhiṁ ?" ॥160
bhaṇiyaṁ vaṇiyasuyā 'amha gurūṇaṁ pi gauravadvāṇaṁ । uggatavacchauyaṁgī ēsā samaṇī samiyapāvā ।। 161 ॥
accabbhuyaṁ ca sāmiṇi । ēyāē māṇasē visālammi । nimmaladēyakaliyammi vi na yahaṁsō paryaṁ kuṇai ॥ 162
dhanā niyaṁti ēyaṁ, dhannā vaṁdanti bhatirāēṇa । dhannā imīē vayaṇaṁ nisuṇaṁti kuṇaṁti ya sayā vi' ॥ 163 ॥
iya sōuṁ savvāhiṁ gaṁtūṇaṁ tāhiṁ vaṁdiyā guruṇī । tīē vi suttavihiṇā dhammakā tāsi pāraddhā ॥ 164 ॥
"dulahaṁ maṇussajammaṁ laddhaṇaṁ rōhaṇaṁ va rōrēṇa । rayaṇaṁ va dhammacaraṇaṁ buddhimayā haṁdi ! vēttavvaṁ ॥ 165 ॥
siddhaṁ pi mahāvijjaṁ asaraṁtō niṣphalaṁ jahā kuṇai । taha dhammapamāilō hāra pattaṁ pi maṇuyattaṁ ॥ 166 ॥
jaha patthaṇālasāṇaṁ ciṁtāmaṇiṇō na dinti dhaṇariddhiṁ । dhammacaraṇālasāṇaṁ taha vihalō maṇuyajammō vi ॥ 167
jaha dulahaṁ kappataruṁ laddhaṁ maggai varāḍiyaṁ mūḍhō । mōkkhaphalē maṇuyattē taha mūḍhō maggaē visara || 168 ॥
tā ginhaha sammattaṁ, paḍivajjaha saṁjamaṁ dhuyāvajjaṁ । tappaha tavaṁ mahaṁtaṁ, jai maggaha jamma-maraṇaṁtaṁ ॥ 169 ॥
chūḍhaṁ saṁjamakōṭṭhē tāvijjaṁtaṁ tavaggiṇā dhaṇiyaṁ । muṁcai kammakalaṁkaṁ jīvasuvanaṁ na saṁdēhō ॥ 170 ॥
dēha dhuvaṁ viṇāsī, tava -saṁjamasāhaṇaṁ phalaṁ tassa । vōlai huliyē jīyaṁ, tā mā dhammē pamāha" ।। 171 ॥
iya gaṇiṇimuhamayaṁkā jhariyaṁ vayaṇāmayaṁ piyaṁtīṇaṁ । micchattavisamasēsa nahaṁ tāsiṁ khaṇadvēṇa ।। 172 ॥
tō tāhiṁ sappamōyaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ “ bhayavai ! na annahā ēyaṁ । jaṁ tumaē āiṭuṁ kiṁtu vayaṁ maṁdasattāō ॥ 173 ॥

'saṁdi maha pahuṇā amhaṁ tumhaṁ ca putrapurisāṇaṁ । iyarajaṇā'sāmannō āsi daḍhaṁ nēhapaḍibaṁdhō ॥। 192 ।।

kō ēttiyaṁ kutō paḍavannaṁ hōjja jai purā tumaē ? । kajjammi sāmasajjhē kō daṁḍaṁ caṁḍamāḍhavaī ? || 310 ।।
ēyārisanibbaṁdhā jai muṇiō maha siṇēhasambhāvō । tā mā māmavamannasu akhaṁḍiō hōi jēṇēsa' ॥ 311 ॥
sōūṇa rāyatrayaṇaṁ saṁvēgarasaṁ paraṁ aṇuhavaṁtī । taṁ paḍibōhiukāmā maṁtipiyā bhaṇiumādattā ॥ 312 ॥
'ēyārisē akajjē ramaṁti jē hōṁti hīṇajāīyā । tumhārisāṇa narapahu ! na hu chajjai ērisaṁ pāvaṁ ।। 313 ॥
na cayai mēraṁ suyaṇō tāvijjaṁtō vi tivvadukkhēṇa । pahaō vi caṁḍamaruyā laṁghai kiṁ sāyarō sīmaṁ ? ॥ 314 ॥
yarisiṇō yatubhēdunnayanāsaṇanimittamiha siṭṭā । sayamētra dunnayarayā kaṇṇalōyaṁ nivārihiha ? || 315 ||
annaṁ ca patthivāṇaṁ avacapāyā payā sadēsatthā । tā tattha pēmarāgō na saṁgaō nāyasārāṇa || 316 ॥
uttamakulajāyāō jāyāō saṁti tē aṇēgāō । lajjasi kiṁ na mahaṁtō hīṇāō mārisitthīō ? ॥ 317 ॥ 25
pōrupayāvapāyavadavapāyaparaṁgaṇāpasaṁgēṇa । mā mā lihasu niratthaṁ ayasapaiṁ satyaṁ (tthiṁ) mayaṁkammi' | 318 ॥
iya sōvavattiyaṁ tīē maṁtiyaṁ saṁtiyaṁ pi mūḍhassa । bhariyaghaḍassa va nīraṁ na tassa kanaṁtarē thakkaṁ ।। 319 ॥
hasiūṇa bhai tō sō “suṁdari ! jāṇāmi nicchiyaṁ savvaṁ । kiṁtu na jujjai ērisaviyāraṇā nēharasiyāṇa || 320.
bhaṇiyaṁ ca-
jētthu gaṇaṁ hi atthu vaijjai, tuccha vi pāṇapīḍa rakkhijjai ।
jētthu ajuttu juttu jōijjai, nēhaha tāsu jalaṁjali dijjai " ॥ 321 ॥
nāūṇa nicchayaṁ sē kaliūṇa ya kālajāvaṇākālaṁ । taṁ buddhivtrayaṁ buddhisuṁdarī sāyaraṁ bhaṇai || 322 ॥
1 vayaṇaṁ khaṁ 1 0 ।। 2 rāyasirijō saṁ1 ॥ 3 paratthaṁ khaṁ ॥ 4 tucchu 2 ॥

pani makāmēṇāvi mēhaṇīsāmiṇā imaṁ vayaṇaṁ । ' mā hujja'sajjhayaṁ bhāmiṇīṇa' paribhāvayaṁtēṇa ॥ 325 ॥

puṇa

vimhiyamaṇēṇa tēṇa vi bhaṇiyaṁ 'tē sāhu suyaṇu ! kōsalaṁ । saccaviyaṁ savisēsaṁ jēṇa imaṁ attaṇō rūvaṁ ॥ 330 ॥
jassa tumaṁ hiyayagayā niyacchamāṇassa tassa phuḍamēyaṁ । nayaṇa-maṇōnivvāṇaṁ suṁdari ! nissaṁsayaṁ kuṇaī' ॥331||
'jai ēvaṁ tā supurisa ! gharēhi ēyaṁ samaṁdirē niccaṁ । muṁcāhi maṁ iyāṇiṁ nibaṁdhaṇaṁ kulakalaṁkassa' ॥ 332 ॥
iya tīē saṁlatē paḍivuttaṁ patthivēṇa 'naṇu ēvaṁ । patraṇēṇa ghaṇā iva jhatti majjha pāṇā vilijjati ॥ 333 ॥
jē tuha saṁgasuhāsārajjunibaddhā duhaṁ maē ruddhā | ghāṁḍēruyasasayā iva abaṁdhaṇā tē palāyaṁti' ॥ 334 ॥
'manē mama saṁgāō ēīē saṁgamō suhaya ! suhaō । ahayaṁ mayaṇaviuttā mayaṇamayā caiva jaṁ ēsā' ॥ 335 ॥
iya biṁtīē tīē utraṇīyā rāiṇō mayaṇamahilā । tēṇa u sāsūyaṁ piva paṇōlliyā pāviyā bhaṁgaṁ ॥ 336 ॥
daṭṭhūṇa asuiniyaraṁ jaṁpara rāyā 'kimērisa muddhē ! । vāḍhaṁ durguchaṇijjaṁ bālāṇa vi cēṭṭhiyaṁ tumaē ?' ॥ 337 ॥
sā bhai 'dēva ! ēsō niyapaḍichaṁdō maē viṇimma viō। ēyārisi cciya ahaṁ ahavā ēttō vi hīṇayarī ॥ 338 ॥
jala-jalaṇāipaōgā sōhijjatō vimujjhaī ēsa। ēyaṁ tu majjha aṁgaṁ naranāha ! na sōhium̐ sakā ।। 339 ॥
asuimmi samuppanaṁ asuissa rasēṇa pāviyaṁ viddhiṁ । atō'mupaḍinaṁ amuī pajjharai savvattō ॥ 340 ॥
jaṁ kira imassa majjhē taṁ jai bāhiṁ pi pāyaḍaṁ hōjjā । kāya-suṇayāṇa tā kō rakkhējja imaṁ sudakkhō vi ? ।। 341
avigaṇiya kulakalaṁkaṁ iya kuhiyakaraṁkakāraṇē kīsa । viyarasi saccaṁkāraṁ taṁ nāraya- tiriyadukkhāṇaṁ ? ॥ 342 ॥
tilatusamētasuhatthē mīṇō iva maṁsapēsiyāluddhō । pāḍēhi appayaṁ mā hu dhīra ! narayānalē ghōrē ॥ 343 ॥
bhuṁjatō paradāraṁ dāraṁ pauṇēi nasyaguttīē । na ya saṁpāvai pāraṁ pāraṁpariyāṇa dukkhāṇaṁ ॥ 344 ॥
kassa na suhaya ! suhāyai saṁgō tumhārisēhiṁ suyaṇēhiṁ ? । kiṁtu na sakā sōḍhuṁ naraē vajjaggijālāō ॥ 345॥
bhōgasuhaṁ maṇuyāṇaṁ saṁjāyai kē parimira divasē । naraē dāruṇadukkhaṁ sāgara - pêliōmāṇēhiṁ ।। 346 ॥
annaṁ ca-
kiṁ pēcchasi mama ahiyaṁ naravara ! aṁtēurāu niyayāō । jaṁ kuṇasi asaggāhaṁ bālō vva anāyaparamatthō || 347॥
avi ya-
maggati vimhiyā jaha ēgaṁ caṁdaṁ jalē jalē bālā । taha tulaṁ bhōgasuhaṁ mūḍhā anannanārīsuṁ" || 348 ॥
iya nisr̥ṇaṁtō sahasā rāyā saṁvēgasāramullavai । 'sāhu subhaṇiyaṁ suṁdari ! nāyaṁ tattaṁ maē dāṇiṁ ॥ 349 ॥

[ 2. 379-
bhaviyanvayāniōyā atakkiyaṁ cētra duddiṇaṁ jāyaṁ । ullā liyakallōla ucchaliō kōliyāvāō ।। 379 ॥
daṭṭhūṇa palayamāruyapahayaṁ va mahōdahiṁ mahābhīmaṁ । ōlaṁbiyā khaṇadvēṇa naṁgarā pōyabhiyagēhiṁ ॥ 380 ॥
saṁkōō siyavaḍō pāraddhā dēvayāṇa vibhattī । vaṇiyamihuṇēṇa vihiyaṁ sāgāraṁ tattha saṁvaraṇaṁ ॥ 381 ॥
bhamiūṇa jāṇavattaṁ cakāiddhaṁ va tātra khaṇamēkaṁ । sīmaṁtiṇihiyayagayaṁ gujjhaṁ pitra takkhaṇē phuṭṭa || 382 ॥
parimukkajīviyāsaṁ buḍḍunibuḍaṇaṁ kuṇatēhiṁ । kaha kaha vi phalayajuyalaṁ suṁdari - dhammēhiṁ saṁpattaṁ ॥ 383 ॥
cau - paṁcavāsarēhiṁ laggāī dō vi ēgadīvammi । miliyāī ca kayāī harisa-visāyaṁ vahaṁtāī ॥ 384 ॥
sulahāō vivayāō, dulahā suvisuddhadhammasaṁsiddhī । iha saṁsārē ghōrē aṇōrapārē samuddē vtra ।। 385 ॥
saṁpattī pamōō na hu juttō āvaīsu ya visāō । jāṇiyaasārasaṁsārarūvajiṇabhaṇiyatattāṇaṁ ॥ 386 ॥
dhīrēhiṁ kāyarēhi ya sōḍhavvamavassamēva suhadukkhaṁ । tamhā dhīrēhiṁ varaṁ sōḍhamiṇaṁ buddhimaṁtēhiṁ ॥ 387 ॥
tē dhīrā sāhasiṇō uttamasattā mahāyasā purisā । āvaigayā vi jē iha na dhammakammē pamāyaṁti ॥ 388 ॥
i anōnnaṁ kasaṇāhiṁ uddhariyadhīrabhāvāī | sāvayadhammaṁ sammaṁ kuṇati tāī pasaṁtāī ॥ 389 ॥
uddhīkayaṁ ca tēhiṁ dīvataḍē bhiṇṇavāhaṇiyaciṁdhaṁ । taṁ pēcchiūṇa pattā tattha narā bēḍiyārūḍhā ॥ 390 ॥
bhaṇiō ya tēhiṁ dhammō lōyaṇavaṇiēṇa pēsiyā amhē । jai ēsi jaṁbudīvaṁ tā āruha ēttha bēḍāē ॥ 391 ॥
tāhē piyāsamēō dhammō taṁ bēḍiyaṁ samārūḍhō । ārōviō ya pōyaṁ sagaurakhaṁ pōyatraṇiṇa || 392 ॥
vaccati bharahasamuhaṁ sannāyakahāhiṁ pamuiyā dō vi । jāva jalanāhakūlaṁ jāyamahōrattadugagammaṁ ॥ 393 ॥
aha dhammabhāriyaṁ hiyayahāriyaṁ lōyaṇō palōyaṁtō । vammahakisaṇukīlākavaliyakāō viciṁtēi ॥ 394 ॥

ahavā-

avirayacāvāyaḍḍhaṇapagāḍhasuḍhiyassa kusumacāvassa । mannāmi itthabhallī jayavijayatthaṁ imā siddhā ॥ 396 ॥
kiṁ jōvvaṇēṇa ? kiṁvā dhaṇēṇa ? kiṁ jīviēṇa rūvēṇa ? | jai mē sayaṁ na laggai ēsā ukkaṁṭhiyā kaṁṭhē || 397
nūrṇa na cētra icchai naramannaṁ niyayabhattukō ēsā । kō pariṇayamāyadaṁ mōttuṁ nivaṣphalaṁ asaī ?" ॥ 398 ॥

tuha saṁtiyaṁ kisōyari ! savvaṁ ciya maha vidattayaṁ ēyaṁ । kiṁ khijjiēṇa saṁpai vihiṇā vihaḍāviē kajjē ? ||404
dāsataṁ pi pavajjiya kāhaṁ maṇanivvuī ahaṁ tujjha । kahasu kimannaṁ saṁpaṛa sakai amhārisō kāuṁ ?' ॥ 405 ॥
iya niyatadullāvā triyakkhaṇā lakkhiūṇa vikkhaṇayaṁ । saṁvēgabhāviyamaṇā niṁdai hiyaē niyaṁ rūvaṁ ॥406 ॥
ciṁtaī “imēṇa nr̥ṇaṁ kayamēyaṁ ērisaṁ mahāpātraṁ । jaṁ rāgaggahagahiyā kajjā - kajjaṁ nē bujjhati ॥ 407 ॥

pariōsāmayarasasittasavvagattēhiṁ niyayamaṇubhūyaṁ । lakkhiyalōyaṇacariyaṁ parōpparaṁ pucchiyaṁ kahiyaṁ ॥ 417 ॥

bhaṇiyaṁ ca 'piē ! dhannā jiṇa - gagahara māiṇō mahābhāgā । jēsiṁ anbhāsatyā cayaṁti jīvā amuhabhāvaṁ |419॥

jēṇasmhaṁ uvayariyaṁ dāviyatīrēṇa ainirīhēṇa । sō vi kaha pēccha pattō jīviyasaṁdēha - dhaṇahāṇi' ।। 421 ॥
iya taṁ sōyaṁtāī tāī diṭṭhāī gāmanāhēṇa । rutramantraṁ tēsiṁ daṭṭhūṇa vircitiyaṁ cētraṁ ॥ 422 ॥
'mayaṇō vva piyāsahiō ēsō khalu kō vi uttamō purisō । vihivilasiēṇa kēṇai ēgāgī iha samāyāō || 423

caliyaṁ ca sē sarīraṁ rasaṁsadōsēṇa thēvadiyahēhiṁ । iya dukuṭṭaniṭṭhāniṭṭhiyacēṭṭhō jiyai kaṭuṁ ॥ 430 ॥

kaiyā kahūṁ va hariyaṁ ? kō si tumaṁ ? kattha tē saputrā haṁ ?' । iya pucchiēṇa baḍuṇā nivēiyaṁ vēiyaṁ niyayaṁ ॥ 502॥
taṁ sōūṇa viciṁtai iṇamō guṇasuṁdarī susaṁviggā । "hī ! garuō aṇubaṁdhō dīsai ēyassa mūḍhassa || 503 ||
gāgaṇī asaraṇā aṇajjamēcchāṇa majjhayārammi । ētō rāgaṁdhāō na yāṇimō 'kaha ṇu chuṭṭissaṁ ? ' ॥ 504 ॥

na hi ēsō vi barāō ēgaṁtēṇētra niraguṇō jēṇa । patthēi nīiniuṇaṁ maḍḍāē khaṁḍai na sīlaṁ || 506 ||

māyā viēttha kajjē pauṁjiyavvā asaṁkahiyayāē । jaṁ pāvajaṇē sadvaṁ unaihaṁ nīisatthēsu" ।। 508 ॥

inhi tu saṁpaōgē lōgē garahā kulassa māliṣṇaṁ । dōggaigamaṇaṁ dāruṇaduhāī bahusō parē lōē ।। 512 ॥
tā paribhāvasu sammaṁ saṁpaikālōciyaṁ mahāsatta ! | pariṇāmasuṁdaraṁ jaṁ, viyārasārā jaō viusā || 513 ॥
nāraṇa jaṁ na siddhaṁ kēsaphalō khalu tayatthamannāō । nihaō caḍaphaḍatō ahiyayaraṁ ghaṁsaṇaṁ lahai" ।। 514 ।।
ēmāitrayaṇarayaṇāraṁjiyacittēṇa ciṁtiyaṁ bahuṇā । 'vināṇabuddhiniuṇā saccaṁ guṇasuṁdarī ēsā ॥ 515 ॥
aivacchalā ya majjhaṁ uvaisai siṇēhasauramii jēṇa । saccaṁ pauṇōvāō kajjassa maē na vināō ॥ 516 ॥
navaraṁ ēyanimittaṁ kaō maē ēttiō parikilēsō । tā kaha muyāmi ēvaṁ pattaṁ bhattaṁ va aichuhiō ? ' ॥ 517 ॥
iya ciṁtiya sā bhaṇiyā 'suṁdari ! savvaṁ pi avitahaṁ bhaṇasi । kiṁtu na tarāmi dhariḍaṁ khaṇaṁ pi pāṇē tuha viōē ॥
jaṁ jīviō mhi suṁdari ! kālaṁ kira ēttiyaṁ tuha viōē । taṁ suyaṇu ! saṁgamāsādivyōsa hisaṁpaōgēṇaṁ ॥ 519 ।।
mailijjaṁtu kulāī, huntu parattha vi duraṁtadukkhāī । parinivyavēhi suṁdari ! tatriyaṁ virahaggiṇā aṁgaṁ' ॥ 520 ॥

niyamaiṇiparāyaṇē kā lajjā ?, ani ya ūsakō ēsō । maṇanēvvuī ya kaha tē hōhī ēttō niyattassa ?' ॥556

bhaṇiō ya suṁdarī 'piyayama ! ēēṇa bhāuṇā ahahyaṁ । jattēga mōiyā rakkhiyā ya krūrāṇa sabarāṇa ।। 558 ।।

"gaṁbhīrima- tuṁgima-mahuravāṇi-rūvāṇi tāva ēēṇa । rayaṇāyara - suragiri-vēgasavāi-mayaṇāṇa gahiyāī ॥ 562 ॥
aṇṇāsaṁbhavi ēvaṁ sōjannaṁ puṇa na yāṇimō kattō । khalasēharē vi jaṁ mārisamma iya pēsalālāvō ॥ 563 ॥

niyagarimaguṇēṇa muṇaṁti nēya khuddāṇa vilasiyaṁ garuyā । nivaḍaṁti taṇōtthayakatriyāsu tuṁgā vi māyaṁgā ॥564
hā ! kaha kaō niratthō maē aṇatthō imassa suyaṇassa ? | phōḍēi birālō lōlayāē sāraṁ pi uttiviḍiṁ ॥ 565॥

niuṇā imīē buddhī jaṁ ēvaṁ pāliyaṁ niyayasīlaṁ । ahahyaṁ pi paḍatō pāvapātraē vāriō vihiṇā || 567 ॥
Tornarāhagahiō jai ēttō nīharējja jīvaṁtō । bhujjō ēvaṁvihadubhaē tā nēva vaṭṭissaṁ " ॥ 568 ॥
aha 'majjaṇavēlā baṭṭaī' tti kiṁkaragaṇēṇa vinnatē । āmaṁtiūṇa iyaraṁ samuṭṭhiō puṇṇasammō vi || 569 ॥

dāūṇa cōkkhajuyalaṁ vihiṇā kayabhōyaṇāikōyavtrā । gamiūṇa diṇaṁ suttā rayaṇīē uciyasējjā ॥ 571 ॥

[ taiō dēvasīha - kaṇayasuṁdarībhavō ]
aha atthi mahimahēlātilaē nilaē sirīṇa sayalāṇaṁ । dēsammi sūrasēṇābhihāṇaē varapurī mahurā ॥ 1 ॥
jā sā pasāhiyā vimalacitēhiṁ hammiēhi dhammiēhi ya, alaṁkiyā bahusāhārēhiṁ bhavaṇēhiṁ ubavaṇēhi ya,
5 ṭiviḍikiyā surayaṇarāyaṁtaṁgaṇēhiṁ nāḍaēhiṁ dhaṇavaipāḍaēhi ya, pavittiyā samunnayasahāvēhiṁ surabhavaṇēhiṁ sajjaṇa-
jaṇēhi ya । jīē ya bhuyaṁgadaṁsaṇaṁ paṇṇavilayānilaēsu, khaluppattī tilajaṁtēsu, daṁḍakaraṇaṁ dhaya-chattēsu, baṁdhaṇaṁ kavva-
kusumē, māraṇaṁ sārijūēsa, karapīḍā jutraisihiṇēsu, khaṁḍaṇaṁ daiyāharēsu, bhaṁḍaṇaṁ muṭṭhiya-taṁbacūḍēsu, bhaṁgō cihurēsu,
maō kuṁjarē, tāsō asuddhamaṇīsu, vaṁcaṇaṁ paharaṇapariguṇiēsu, paradāragamō bhikkhāyarēsu, dōjīhattamuragēsu, guṇa-
hāṇī charsary cēva lakkhijjaiti ।
10 tī varanayarīē mayaraddhaya-dhaṇaya kēsarisaricchō । rūtra ppayārṇai- pōrusaguṇēhiṁ mēhō nikō hōtthā ॥ 2 ॥
bhayamappaṇī asataṁ ēgamaṇēgāṇa vīravērīṇaṁ । ditēṇa jēṇa jugavaṁ jaṇāṇa jaṇiyaṁ mahācōjjaṁ ॥ 3 ॥
tāviyapatrikkhēṇa vi jassa payāvēṇa vittharaṁtēṇa । parinivyaviyā niyadēsavāsiṇō payaisaṁdōhā ॥ 4 ॥
tassa ya vimalasuvittā guruguṇasārā maṁgōharāyārā । muttāvali vva suhayā dēvī muttāvalī nāma ॥ 5 ॥
tīē vijjujjalaviggahāē ujjōiō kulanahammi । rēhai mēhō mēhō va dāṇasalilēga varisaṁtō ॥ 6 ॥
are hiyayagayāē nicaṁ vijjāharī va vijjāē । mēhō mahaṁtanēhō karēi kiccāī savvāī ॥ 7 ॥

274] dēvasēṇa caṁdakaṁtāṇaṁ pavvajjā dēvalōgagamaṇaṁ ca । taō piyaṁkaracakki maisāgaramaṁtittēṇōvavannāṇaṁ nivvāṇaṁ ।
annayā ya suyasāgarāṇagāraṁtiē nisāmiūṇaṁ saṁsārāsārayaṁ, macchu-jarā-ruyāṇaṁ ca dunivārayaṁ, visayāṇa vira-

rāyā,
tāhē piyaṁkaranariṁdō samāsāiyacakkāimahārayaṇō pasāhiyasayalabhārahō battīsamahāsāmaṁtasahassamatthayālimālā-

nō māyaṁgā na caṁgā turayarahavarā nētra sāmaṁtajōhā, bhaṁḍāgāraṁ na sāraṁ na rayaṇanihiṇō nētra dvārā udārā ।
nahaṁ gēyaṁ na tāraṁ taha maṇaharaṇaṁ nēya rajjaṁ na rahūṁ, diṭṭhō ruṭṭhō vi tuṭṭhi jaha aha sacivō rāiṇō sē karēi ॥ 253 ॥
maṁtī vinivaṁ mannai dēvaṁ va guruṁ va niddhabaṁdhuṁ va । hiyayaṁ ca lōyaṇaṁ pitra santrastaṁ jīviyaṁ va sayā ॥ 254 ॥
sa fresparōpparanēhamhiyā annayā duvēhaṁ pi । kāraṇajinnāsāē jāyā ciṁtā aśmahaṁtā || 255 ॥
'hōyavtramamha nūṇaṁ parabhavasaṁbaṁdhiṇā siṇēhēṇa । na hi sāmi - sēvagāṇaṁ pīī ēvaṁvihā ghaḍai ॥ 256 ॥
ar as kahiṁ pi katthai pēcchāmō divvanāṇiṇaṁ kiṁ pi । tā taṁ pucchiya karimō vinicchyaṁ ēttha vatthummi' ॥
iya ciṁtirāṇa tēsiṁ saṁsayasaṁtamasa nirasaṇadinim̐dō । suragaṇamahiō tahiyaṁ samāgaō suppahajinim̐dō ॥ 258 ॥
muttōūlapalaṁbiyaphalihaphuraṁtō rukiraṇajālēṇa । chattattaēṇa suiṇā rēhaṁtō niyajasēṇēva ॥ 259 ॥
pēlatō tamaniyaraṁ samaṁtaō niyayataṇusamutthēṇa । bhāmaṁḍalēṇa mahayā muttimayā kēvalēṇaṁ ca ॥ 260 ॥
puraō calaṁtacāmara - siṁhāsaṇa cakka - ciṁdharudva hō । ugghuṭujayapahuttō duṁduhiṇā tārasaddēṇa ॥ 269 ॥

vaddhātrayapurisāō sōuṁ taṁ dō vi pamuiyā dhaṇiyaṁ । sīyaṁtachēttavāsaṁta kāliyā rōrasaṇiya vva ॥ 263 ॥

tō kāū paṭṭha vihiṇā rōmaṁcacacciyasarīrō । anyēbhūyaṁ pūyaṁ paidiyahaṁ kāumāraddhō ॥ 317 ॥

5 hidiyasayalasattāō mahāmahantajattāō, kārēi micchattavāhipasamaṇāī rahaniggamaṇāī, nivvattēi pupphagaṁdhāibhōgā-

1

jiṇasāhu- vēiyāṇaṁ bhattaṇurattō pabhāvaṇujjuttō । jāō jaṇō asēsō tasē tayaṇumāṇēṇa ॥ 319 ॥

'juttamiyāṇiṁ mama nimmamassa sāmannamuttamaṁ cariḍaṁ । gihidhammakappataruṇō phalamēyaṁ caiva jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 321॥
kiṁtu na ajja vi rajjōrubhāradharaṇammi paccalō kumarō । tēṇa na tarāmi caiuṁ ēyaṁ daḍhanēhabaṁdhavasō || 322 ॥
ahavā imassa rajjaṁ dāum̐ paricattarajjavāvārō । ciṭṭhāmi dhammaniraō jā ēsō pāvai paṭṭaṁ || 323 ॥
tōliyaniyasāmatthō saṁjamabhāraṁ ta gharissāmi । pariṇāmasuṁdaramiṇaṁ ēvaṁ ciya hōi kīraṁtaṁ' ॥ 324 ॥

jaṁ divrahō rammō diṭṭhō sumiṇē imassa jaṇaṇīē । tā dēvarahō nāmaṁ vālassa paiṭṭhiyaṁ piuṇā ॥ 18 ॥

iya pariyāṇi tattō rāyā viyasaṁtatrayaṇasayatrattō । rōmaṁcaciyagattō kumaraṁ paṛa bhaṇiumādattō ॥ 89 ॥
'bhō ! sāhu raṇē ramiyaṁ payāsiyaṁ vimalakittikulagayaṇaṁ । nāsiyamamhāṇa tamaṁ dēvarahakumāra ! sūra! tumē ' ॥90॥
ētyaṁtarē pavajjiyāī vaddhāvaṇayatūrāī, paghōsiyā udāmasadaṁ baṁdiṇō, nāyaparamatthā ya vimhiyā savvē rāya-
kumārā mōiyā baṁdhaṇāō kayasāhāviyāgārēṇa kumārēṇa । tē tri 'sōhaṇamiṇaṁ, jaṁ vimalakittiattayammi nivaḍiyā
varamāla ' ti jaṁpatā paṭṭamuhapaṁkayā paṇamiūṇa khāmiūṇa ya kumāraṁ tagguṇukittaṇēkavāvārā paḍigayā sahāṇēsu ।
rayagāvī vipariōsarasamauntramaṇuhavaṁtī kulakamāgayavihiṇā vivāhiyā kumārēṇa ।
unbhūyaputrapēmō tuṭṭō kumarō vi tīē lābhēṇa । kassa na jāyai tōsō ahavā rayaṇāvalīlā ? ॥ 91 ॥
ravitēō vi pamuiō aṇurūtravarēṇa niyayadhūyāē । dēvara hē rayaṇāvalisaṁjōgō kaṁ na tōsēi ? ॥ 92 ॥
'aṇurūtrō saṁjōgōṁ, dhannā kaṣnā, barō vi kayapuṣnō । sōhaggakapparukkhō imēhiṁ cinnō tavō nūṇaṁ ॥ 93 ॥
saṁgasuṁdarī vā sammaṁ ārāhiō tavō puvvi' । iyaullāvakkhaṇiō jāō nāyarajaṇō sancō ।। 94 ॥
jaṇamaṇa - lōyaṇasuhaō suhamacchiya tattha vāsarē kēi । ladvāṇumnō kumarō caliō niyapuravariṁṇa ॥ 95 ॥
syaṇāvalī virayaṇāvalīhiṁ vivihāhiṁ maṁḍiyāvayavā । bahurkikarīsamēyā vidinnagaya- turaya rahavūhā ।। 96 ॥
vivipaḍivattiniuṇaṁ visajjiyā patthivēṇa saṁcaliyā । bāhajalōlakabōlā muhu muhu nayaraṁ nihālitī ||97||
aha vacatō kumarō daiyāē sōyajalaṇasamaṇatthaṁ । dāvēi kōuyāīṁ vivihāī rannamajjhami ॥ 98 ॥
katthai pullī ārūḍhapahiyatarumūlakhaṇaṇa akkhaṇitō । rōsaṁdhō na hi lakkhai sēnnaṁ āsannattaṁ pi ।। 99 ।।
katthai avaccanēhēṇa hariṇaō gahiyasāvayaṁ vagghaṁ । rōsuppittha siṁgēhi haṇai vēgēṇa vaccaṁta ॥ 100 ॥

pi ēttha bahumāṇō' tti bahuvihamaṇusāsiūṇa suṁē gayā annattha sāhuṇō ।

sūiyattēṇa kayasyaṇasihābhihāṇō suhēṇa pattō sukayakalākalāvōvalaṁbhaṁ jōvvaṇāraṁbhaṁ । pariṇāviō ya piuṇā kumāra-

asthi samuddammi va mahālacchinivāsē mahōdaya bharasuṁdarē ya vijayaurē nayarē sūrassa va bahutamārividdhaṁsaṇō-

15 ciṁtāmaṇī atthisatthassa, vajjapaṁjaraṁ saraṇāgayāṇaṁ, ammāpiyaraṁ dīna-duhiyāṇaṁ, ūsaradharaṇī dubhayadhannāṇaṁ । tassa

jāō saṁlāvō 'gaṁtūṇa saṁtaraṁ karēmō niyapunnaparicchaṁ' । 'kahaṁ puṇa jaṇayāṇi muccissaṁti ?" ti uvāyamaggaṇujja-

97
cārissāmi, jēṇa mama sāmisālanayarē asuhagaṁdhō na hōi, samappēhi vā taṁ mahārayaṇaṁ' । rāiṇā vr̥ttaṁ 'mitta ! kērisaṁ

[ 5.14-
ṭhaviyaṁ ca tassa suviṇāṇusāraō sammaēṇa baṁdhūṇaṁ । nāmaṁ jaṇābhirāmaṁ suvāsarē punnacaṁdōti ॥ 14 ॥

17 ॥
vaṇī kalākalāvē kīlai paṇhōttarāikavvēhiṁ । kuṇai viṇōyaṁ gaṁbhīrabhāvapatthāvapāḍhē ।। 16 ।।
5 lajjara jūyakahāē, untriya vilāsiṇīṇa vatāē । na saha nāmaṁ mahu-majja-maṁsa- pāra dvigiddhāṇaṁ ॥
aha rayaṇāvalidēvō dīvō iva patraṇapēlliō sahasā । cattasarūvō caviḍaṁ tattō kira dēvalōgāō ॥ 18 ॥

jayādēvīē, tā ēhi turiyaṁ, na tuha muhayaṁdālōyaṇaṁ viṇā dēvī gāsaggahaṇaṁ karēi' । tti sōūṇa 'jamāṇavē aṁba' tti

'piyasahi ! caṁdakalaṁ pi hu pēcchaṁtāṇaṁ avēi saṁtāvō | kaha tuha pavaḍhiō sō palōiē punacaṁdē vi ?' || 57॥
annāē bhannai--
5
'pasamēi na saṁtāvaṁ daṁsaṇamēttēṇa punacaṁdō vi । avi ya phusaṁtō aṁgaṁ samaṁtaō kōmalakarēhiṁ ' ॥ 58 ॥
chēyamaṇiyāṇi tāsi niṇaṁtī pupphasuṁdarī ēvaṁ । īsiṁavēyahiriyā vilakkhahasirī taō bhai ॥ 59 ॥
' ḍhaiyarō vi paḍichalijjai, avi baṁcijjai jamō vi niuṇēṇa । gōvaṁtī vi hu bhāvaṁ tarāmi na hi vaṁciuṁ tubbhē ॥
sayalā vi maṇōvittī paccakkhā tumha jōgiṇīṇaṁ va । tā kahaha ihōvāyaṁ ēgēṇa vi akkhavattēṇa ' ॥ 61 ॥
iyarīhiṁ taō vuttaṁ "maipasarī amha kērisō muddhē ! | saihapaṁsukī liyāē jaṛa tuha cittaṁ na lakkhēmō 1 ॥ 62 ॥ 10
jaṁ puṇa pucchasi suṁdari ! maṇasaṁtāvassa pasamaṇōvāyaṁ । tattha vi suṇāhi tattaṁ pacakkhaṁ amha jaṁ vittaṁ ॥ 63॥
kallaṁ khu piyaṁgumaṁjarīdēvīē tuha tāyassa saṁlāvō saṁvr̥ttō 'kaha nāma puṇphasuṁdarī kumārapunnacaṁdēṇa saṁjōiyantra ?'ti ।
taō bhaṇiyaṁ tuha jaṇaēga-
15
'uciō imīē kumarō mauḍō iva bhaiṇi ! uttamamaṇīē । cūḍāmaṇi va pahumatthayassa ēsā vi sē uciyā ॥
gōharaṇa niuttā kaṇayāharaṇārihā varamaṇi vya । amnaniuttā ēsā jaṇē jagayāṇa uvahāsaṁ ॥ 65 ॥
ēsō vi amnanārīniōiō pāunēi na cchāyaṁ । majjārigala piṇaddhō navaghaḍiō kaṇayadōrō vva ॥ 66 ॥
kiṁtu na dīsara ēsiṁ rāgavigārō maṇē maṇāgaṁ pi । na sahati jēṇa dōnni vi vīvāhaka parēsiṁ pi ॥ 67 ॥
na hasaṁti payaḍadaṁtaṁ, siṁgārakahāhiṁ na ya rasijjati । na kuṇaṁti kēlikalahaṁ jayaṁti na viddhavayaṇāī ॥ 68 ॥
tō na hi najjai ēsiṁ hōjja na vā niviḍanēhasaṁbaṁdhō । tēṇa u viṇā vivāhō tavai sayā nasalaṁ va ॥ 69 ॥
asthi ya jaṇē patrāō sarisasahāvāṇa hōi kira pēmaṁ । iya ēyāṇa vi kaiyā vi hōjja jammaṁtaranimittā ||70 || 20
tā kīraṁtu imēsiṁ parōpparaṁ tātra daṁsaṇullāvā । jēhiṁ kalijjai sajjō sunicchiō kajjaparamatthō' ॥ 71 ॥
tō dēvīē bhaṇiyaṁ 'ēvamiṇaṁ bhāi ! jaṁ tumaṁ bhaṇasi । jaha nāmēṇa tahēva hi buddhīi vi taṁ visālō si' ॥72॥
kahiūṇa tattamamhaṁ jaṇaṇī - jaṇaēhiṁ ajja dōhiṁ pi । ujjāṇadaṁsaṇatthaṁ diṣṇō tumhārṇamāsō ॥ 73 ॥
sahi ! saṁpunnā ajjaṁ maṇōrahā tumha jaṇaṇi-jaṇayāṇaṁ । pujjissaṁti lahuṁ ciya tujjha vi, vaddhāvaṇaṁ dēsu" ॥74॥
ēyaṁ sahīvayaṇamāyaniūṇa jāyā maṇāgaṁ nivvuyahiyayā rāyaduhiyā । ēvaṁ ciya kumārō vi nibbuīkaō 25
niyamitēhiṁ | anōnakōsalliyapēsaṇaviṇōēṇa ya pavōliyā vāsarā । dinā ya pasatyatihi-karaṇamuhuttē visālasāmaṁ-
tēṇa sabahumāṇaṁ puṣphasuṁdarī puna yaṁdakumārassa | sīhasēṇarāiṇā vi kāriō puravarīē paramāṇaṁdō । taō-
gurumuravaga hiraguṁjiyanaccaṁta sihaṁḍiruiragharasiharaṁ । siharārūḍha puraṁgaṇa muhapaṁkayama hiyasurabhavaṇaṁ ।। 75 ।।
bhavaṇaṁgaṇapauraṁgaṇaniuruṁba vihijjamāṇavaranahaṁ । naṭṭāvajjiyanaravara dijjaṁtāharaṇakayasōhaṁ ॥ 76 ॥

kūḍatula- kūḍamāṇa- tappaḍirūvabhaṁḍēhiṁ । tahā vina suṭhu lahai - vasudattōti । payaṭṭā gahiyatahāvihappamullabhaṁḍā puṁḍauraṁ ।
iō ya tanayarasāmiṇā vasutēyanarāhivēṇa avacayaṁ kaṁci bhaṇḍāgāriyaṁ licchaṁtēṇa paricchānimittaṁ niuttā
paccaiyamaṇussā mahagghābharaṇāṇi maggēsu ṭhaviūṇa pattaladumasālānilukā nihālaṁtā cidvaṁti । gahiukāmaṁ ca kaṁci
daṇa mahayā saddēṇa khaṁkāriti । aō na kōi tāī giṇhai । ginhataṁ ca 'takaraṁ ' ti kariya daṁḍati । taōva
20 vaṇiṇō ēttha sarayadiṇayarabhāsuraṁ puraō maṇikuṁḍalaṁ pāsaṁti । taō 'ahō ! sayaṁvarā siri' tti jaṁpatō valiō
tayabhimu vasudattō । 'naṇu hālāhalaṁ visamēyaṁ' ti ciṁtēṇa vāriō iyarēṇa niyattiūṇa ya vaikaṁtō dūrēṇa । tassa
bōṇatthaṁ siddhō titō māidattēṇa, jahā -
[ 3. dēva - jasavaṇiyaditō ]
kira amha nayarē dēvō jasō ya dō vaṇiyā sāhāraṇatravahāriṇō ahēsi । dēvō sāvaō adimnaṁ na giues,
25 iyarassa natthi niyamō । annayā viyārabhūmīō niyattamāṇēhiṁ dinaṁ maggāsanē nivaḍiyaṁ kaṇayakuṁḍalaṁ । dēvēṇa vaya-
bhaṁgabhīruṇā na nihāliyaṁ pi । jasēṇa tallajjāē tayātrahīriyaṁ pi maggaṁtarēṇa gaṁtūṇa saṁgōviyaṁ, ciṁtiyaṁ ca 'mahāṇubhāvō
dēvō jassērisī alōbhayā, tahā vi ēyasāhāraṇamiṇaṁ karissāmi' |
amnayā nayaraṁtarāō taṁ ca amnaṁ ca sāhāraṇabhaṁḍaṁ viṇiōiūṇamāṇiyamaṇēṇa pabhūyaṁ paḍibhaṁḍaṁ । kayā dēvēṇa
āya-vyayanirūvaṇā । 'pabhūyaṁ paḍibhaṁḍaṁ' ti saviyakkēṇa pucchiō jasō । jāhē sō annamannāī vāgarē tāhē sahasā -
30 viō kāūṇa savisēsaṁ pucchiō । kahiē sambhāvē niddhāriūṇa nīṇiyamāvaṇāō ahiyaṁ bhaṁḍaṁ saṁgōviyaṁ jasēṇa niya-
maṁdirē | navaraṁ tīē cēva rayaṇīē khattaṁ dāūṇa taṁ ca amnaṁ ca avahariyaṁ takkarēhiṁ । visamnō jasō bhaṇiō dēvēṇa 'mitta !

annāyāgayadhaṇamaṇatthanibaṁdhaṇaṁ cēva hōi, tā karēhi saṁpayaṁ tannivitti' । abbhuvagayamiṇaṁ jasēṇa । duiyadivasē samāgayā

tā bhadda ! nāyuvajjaṇē jayavvaṁ kimēiṇā pariṇāmatrirasēṇa cōraṁkārahēuṇā paradhaṇagahaṇēṇaṁ ? ti । ēvamuttō

karēhi amda pasāyaṁ' ti ciṁtēhiṁ saviṇayaṁ nīō rāyamaṁdiraṁ । daṁsiō nariṁdassa । nivēiō kuṁḍaladaṁsaṇāivaiyarō |

kahiyā niyamagahaṇavattā । taō tuṭṭhēṇa rāiṇā dinaviulajīvaṇō niuttō bhaṁḍāgārē ēsō jāō mahiḍiō
savtrajaṇasammaō ya । vaḍṁtaguru bahumāṇō bhaddayabhāvamaṇuhaviūṇa samāhiṇā kayadēhacāō jāō ihēva vijaē caṁdā-

'ahō ! avivēgaviyaṁbhiyaṁ'ti bhāvarīē diṭṭhidāṇamēttēṇāvi aṇāsāsiēhiṁ tēhiṁ bhūriritthavvaraṇa uvayariyā kāi

'dhammō jiṇēhiṁ kahiō savvajiyāṇaṁ dayāvihāṇēṇa । tēsu duhiē suṁdari ! tā kuṇasu dayaṁ payattēṇa' ॥136॥

parivvāigāē 'bhaddā ! muyaha tayaggahaṁ jai suhaṁ jīvitamicchaha' । tahā vi aniyattaggahēhiṁ tēhiṁ ārāhiō maṁtasiddhō ।
tēṇāvi kasiudasirattīē nīyā tē nayarujjāṇaṁ । ālihiyaṁ maṁḍalagaṁ । pūiūṇa tammajjhōvaidvēṇa pāraddhō maṁta-

kārasaraṇaparāyaṇā jāva ciṭṭhai, tāva bhaṇiyā tē siddhēṇa 'arē ! samāgayā ēsā tumha daiyā, karēha jaṁ vō rōyaha'

caitra pahāyā rayaṇī । diṭṭhō sō vaiyarō nayarajaṇēṇa । paraṁparāē samuppanakōugā miliyā nayasppahāṇā । samāgaō
sayaṁ sūrarāyā । paccabhināyā jaṇēṇa tē suṁdarī ya । 'kō ēsa vaiyarō ?' tti pucchiyaṁ nariṁdēṇa । jāhē na taraṁti
jaṁpiuṁ dullaliyā, suṁdarī vi'na yāṇāmi' tti jaṁpatī lajjōṇayā ciṭṭhai tāhē abhayaṁ jāiūṇa sāhiō paramatthō

'jō thēvasaṁpayāē kayakicaṁ muṇai appayaṁ purisō । kuviō tassa kayaṁtō na dēi nūṇaṁ siriṁ ahiyaṁ । 155 ।।
saccamēyaṁ, kamanahā ēsa tihuyaṇalacchiaṁchēṇapaḍihatthabhrayadaṁḍō imassa muṁḍatuṁḍassa bōllēhiṁ lahuṁ caiva saṁkōiya-

lābhō । tahā vi bahuralābhahēuṁ gaō parayaradēsaṁ । tattha vi saṁpattapaṭṭasuyāimahagghapaḍibhaṁḍō paḍiniyatttō pattō
ēgaṁ mahāḍaviṁ । tātraya pajjaliō palayaggivibbhamō dāvānalō । taō pāṇabharaṇa palāṇō samaṁtēṇa bhiyagavaggō ।

dēvī va tivvatavatāvavisōsiyaṁgī, ārāhiūṇa maraṇaṁtavihiṁ visuddhaṁ ।
tatthēva dēvanilaē surapuṁgavattaṁ, pattā'kalaṁkagihidhammanisēvaṇēṇa ।। 178 ॥
ēgamarammē milē vimāṇē, tē dō vi dēvā daḍhanē baddhā ।

[ chaṭṭhō sūrasēṇa-muttāvalībhavō ]
5
punnāṇubaṁdhipunnappabaṁdhasaṁbaṁdhasutthiyā suiraṁ । vasiūṇa cuyā tattō saṁpattā jaṁ tayaṁ suṇaha ॥ 1 ॥
asthi vidēhādēsō dāhiṇabharahadramajjhimē khaṁḍē । viyaraṁtadīhabhuyagōvasōhiō nāgalōgō vva ॥ 2 ॥
tattha ya unakōṭṭā vicittapattā subhōgiāhārā । mihilāpurī pasiddhā ghaṇamuiyā mōramutti vva ॥ 3 ॥
paramahilā paramahilā vi jattha hiyayaṁ jaṇāṇa nō harai । na rayapayaṁ narayapayaṁ ti bhāvirāṇaṁ sarīraṁ sē ॥ 4 ॥
jattha ya sanaccaṇāī jiṇacaṇāī jaṇō niyacchaṁtō । viṁdai paramāṇaṁdaṁ suramāṇaṁ daṁsayaṁtō vva ॥ 5 ॥
dīsaṁti sayā rāmā aṁtō bāhiṁ ca jattha suvisatthā । aṁtō natthi viruddhō, dīsai bāhiṁ tarusamūhō ॥ 6 ॥
tī nayarīē dariyāridaṁtikēsarī taruṇinaliṇībiyāsaṇēkkaṇēsarī baṁdhukumuyapunimāyaṁdō asthisatthavihaga-
kamāyaṁdō duṭṭhakaṁṭhīravasarahō niyapayāvakaṁtaviulabharahō aputtavittanirīhō rāyā narasīhō sāmittamaṇuhavai । atriya - 10
jasa- kittipakkhapasaraṁ apāyamāṇassa rāyahaṁsassa । aimaḍahapaṁjaraṁ pitra bhāsai bhuvaṇattayaṁ jassa ॥ 7 ॥
tasya sarasī va baṁgālīṇa sārasōhā, rāyahaṁsi vva visuddhōbhayapakkhā, mērumēhalā iva saittamālavaṇā,
gaṁgā iva saralasacchasahāvasārataraṁgā, dūrāvaginadōsajālā guṇamālā nāma mahādēvī ।
15
saṁpunnamahābhōgaṁ aparakaṁtaṁ mahiṁ paṇaiṇi ca । utrarbhujaṁtō jaṁtaṁ na mugai kālaṁ nariṁdō sō ॥ 8 ॥
aha anadinē parikkasaṁṭhiō cauracārapurisēṇa । viṇayapaṇaēṇa niuṇaṁ viśvaviō sō mahīnāhō ॥9॥
“dēva ! maē puracāraṁ nirūvamāṇēṇa vāvisaraṇīē । purasuṁdarīṇa nisuō ajja navallō samullāvō ॥ 10 ॥
pakkhuliyāē bhaṇiyaṁ ēgāē 'jiyau rāyanarasīhō' । amnā bhaṇai 'na sīhō ēsō narajaṁbuō muddhē ! ॥ 11 ॥
jō puttarayaṇarahiyaṁ appāṇaṁ pēṁcchirō vi appāṇaṁ । bhuṁjai suvai visatthō na pauṁjai vikamujjōyaṁ ॥ 12 ॥
jēmaṁta - jōya - vijjāviyakkhaṇā sayalasiddhipēḍihatthā । tē garuḍassa va ahiṇō imassa āṇaṁ na laṁghēti ॥ 13 ॥
vāyāmēttēṇa samīhiyāī sijyaṁti jassa sēsāī । taha vi parakamarahiō kiṁ na halā ! jaṁbuō ēsō ? " ॥ 14 ॥ 20
iccāi cittavattaṁ sōūṇa carā narīsarō sahasā । suyalābhatthī maṁtīṇa maṁḍalaṁ pucchara uvāyaṁ ।। 15 ॥
tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ 'mahāpahu ! subbai iha cōjjaḍaṁbarō jōī। saṁpai pattō sattō samatthajaṇapatthiyatthē ॥ 16 ॥
sō dēva ! sōvayāraṁ maggajjau naṁdaṇaṁ kimaśrēṇa ? । iyagaruyakajjabharadhuradhuraṁdharō nāvarō bhuvaṇē' ॥ 17 ॥
sōūṇa vayaṇamēyaṁ āhūō takkhaṇēṇa sō ramnā । pattō ya sahāmajjhaṁ gajjatō mattadaṁti vva ॥ 18 ॥

puhavīcaṁdacariē chaṭē sūrasēṇa muttāvalōbhavē
[ 6.19-
pavarāsaṇōvaviṭṭhō kayasakkārō nivēṇa saṁlattō । 'jōiṁda ! kahasu kēttiyamēttaṁ sāmatthamuvvahasi ? ' ॥ 19 ॥
īsi hasiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ tēṇa 'mahīnāha ! kimiha pucchāē ? | āisa kajjaṁ sajjō saṁpāijjau jamēttāhē ॥ 20 ॥
kiṁ nāgakanyāō āṇēmi basē ? uyāmarabahūō ? | aha dubairicakaṁ paṇaī kārēmi calaṇēsu ? || 21 ॥
gaya-turayarayaṇamahavā dūratthaṁ jhatti ajja āṇēmi ? । annaṁ pi kiṁ pi visamaṁ paōyaṇaṁ bhaṇasu sāhēmi' ॥ 22 ॥
'jai ēvaṁ tā jōiṁda ! kōugaṁ ēkamamha pūrēhi । āṇēhi nāgarāyassa piyayamaṁ ēttha atthāṇē ' ॥ 23 ॥
iya naravaraṇā bhaṇiē samāhimāpūriūṇa turiēṇa । āṇīyā tārāharaṇahāriṇī tēṇa divvitthī ॥ 24 ॥
papphullavayaṇakamalā kayakaramaulā samuddhasiyarōmā । 'āisaha 'tti bhaṇaṁtī ṭhiyā ya sā jōiṇō puraō ||25||
tēṇāvi 'suyaṇu ! kuṇa naravaissa āṇaṁ'ti bhaṇiyamēttāē । tīai vr̥ttō narasīhapatthivō 'sāmi ! āisaha' ॥26॥
ranā bhaṇiyaṁ 'suṁdari ! kā si tumaṁ ? kaha ṇu āgayā ēttha ?' । tīē bhaṇiyaṁ “ nāgiṁdapaṇaiṇī ṇāgalōyāō ॥ 27
tēlōkākhaṁḍiya sāsaṇassa ēyassa jōgiṇō vayaṇā । patta mhi tumha parisaṁ 'kahaṁ ?' ti sammaṁ na yāṇāmi " ॥ 28 ॥
tō jāyajō jaṁpiyapaccayamaivimhiēṇa namiūṇa | ramnā visajjiyā sā gayā ya ahaṁsaṇaṁ sahasā ।। 29॥
'avvō ! mahappabhāvō jōiṁda ! tumaṁ' ti saṁlavaṁtēṇa । kāūṇa vivittaṁ niyapaōyaṇaṁ sāhiyaṁ tō sē ॥ 30 ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ ca tēṇa 'naravai ! kēttiyamēyaṁ paōyaṇaṁ majjha ? । saṁtinasāyarāṇaṁ kā ciṁtā gōpauttaraṇē ? ॥ 31 ॥
navaraṁ hōsu sahāō kasiṇacaudasinisāi ēgāgī । sakkhaṁ jāliṇidēviṁ jēṇa davāvēmi tē puttaṁ ॥ 32 ॥
ahavā na puttayaṁ ciya dāhaṁ jammaggiyaṁ tuhaṁ savvaṁ । tumha pabhāvā majjha vi aṇuggahō tīē siddhī' ॥ 33 ॥
natramēhagajjiraṁ taṁ sōūṇa nariṁdavarahiṇō hihō । paḍivajjiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ pūittu tayaṁ visajjēi ॥ 34 ॥
muṇiyasamaēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ maṁtīhiṁ 'nariṁda ! suṁdarī maṁtō। kiṁtu na vīsasiyanvaṁ ēgatēṇērisajaṇassa ॥ 35 ॥
rakkhēyavbō appā sappāō iva imāō jattēṇa । cittacariyā hu jīvā havaṁti kammāṇa vēhammā' || 36 ॥
paḍivannamaṁtivayaṇō kasiṇacaudasi nisāpaōsammi । pattō tassa samīvaṁ khaggasahāō mahārāō || 37 ॥
pattā ya tē masāṇaṁ saṁkēyagihaṁ va aṁdhatamasāṇaṁ । rōlaṁtanarakaraṁkaṁ kāyaraukaṁpaṇakaraṁkaṁ ॥ 38 ॥
katthai ruddagharaṁ piva dīsaṁtala saṁtasivaisivārūvaṁ । amnattha khēḍayaṁ pitra sacchaṁda bhamaṁtavēyālaṁ ॥ 39 ॥
haranāḍayaṁ va katthas pisāyaaṭṭaṭṭahāsabībhacchaṁ | annattha raṇagaṇamitra alaṁghavasa - maṁsahikkāsaṁ ॥ 40 ॥
sammajjiūṇa dharaṇī ciyaggidīvēṇa maṁḍalālihaṇaṁ । pāraddhaṁ jōīdēṇa patthivō puṇa imaṁ vr̥ttō ॥ 41 ॥
'atthēttha dāhiṇēṇaṁ naggōhatarussa putrasāhāē । ubbaddhagō maṇussō āṇēhi tayaṁ asaṁbhaṁtō ॥ 42 ॥
subahuṁ pi jaṁpamāṇassa tassa paḍiuttaraṁ na dāyavvaṁ । na ya kaissai bhētavyaṁ āgaṁtavyaṁ turaṁtēṇa ' ॥ 43 ॥
aha tattha gaō rāyā sāhaṁ āruhiya chiṁdaē pāsaṁ । ōinō ya nihālai taṁ lavaṁtaṁ tahiṁ caiva ॥ 44 ॥
ēka dui pi vāraṁ, tāhē sāhāgaō vi gahiūṇaṁ । tōḍiyapāsō sahasā ōimnō paḍiniyattō ya ॥ 45 ॥
taṁ jaṁpara vēyālō sahiō 'tamasi mūḍha ! sēyālō । mōttūṇa khattadhammaṁ karēsi iya kucchiyaṁ kammaṁ ॥ 46 ॥
aṇuharasi rakkhasāṇaṁ hiṁḍatō ratimērisamasāṇaṁ । hīṇō si nihīṇāṇa vi chivamāṇō parakaraṁkāī ॥ 47 ॥

aṅkaḥ - utsaṅgō yasya" ॥ 5 saṁkēta:- "śinvitaṁ - rudrānvitaṁ śivāyāḥ - gauryā rūpam aśivam- amaṅgalabhūtaṁ śivārūpaṁ yatra ॥ 6 "bhaprā

yatra " ॥ 9 dharaṇi jē0 vinā ॥। 10 asthittha jē0 vinā ॥। 11 kalaya mēyadhvaṁ jē0 ॥ 12 " grāmyaḥ " khaṁraṭi● ॥

puttakaṁkhinarasīhanivakrayaṁ cōjaḍaṁbarā hihāṇajōiṁdassa uttarasāhagattaṁ, kubuddhijōiṁdapaḍibōhō ya ।
127
taṁ tēṇa duṭṭapāsaṁḍiēṇa kāūṇa khaṁḍakhaṁḍāī । kīrasi bhūyāṇa balī jai muṁcasi maṁ na cāhē ' ॥ 48 ॥
iyajaṁpirēṇa daṁsiyavihīsiyāsaya sahassarūvēṇa । akhuhiyacittō vr̥ttō nivō puṇō tudr̥ḍhēyarēṇaṁ ॥ 49 ॥
“bhō ! sāhu sāhasaṁ tē sārō paḍivamnanicchaō vaccha ! । tuṭṭhō bhaṇāmi sacaṁ ētthamahaṁ sattavāyāō ॥ 50 ॥
taṁ suyakāmī, sō dusāhagō caṣphalō phuḍaṁ bujjha । saccamiṇaṁ ' vaṁcijjai luddhō aliyappalāvīhiṁ' ॥ 51 ॥
dāūṇa bali sō tuha sarīrayaṁ mahai sāhiuṁ amhē । iya iṁdiyālanārīdaṁsaṇaō taṁ si akkhittō ॥ 52 ॥
tā mā kiliksa naravara ! tujjha suō sattarattamajjhammi । hōhī avassamēva hi nivēitō sūrasumiṇēṇa ॥ 53 ॥
paḍivanasārayāē mayagamiṇaṁ jai vi nēhi taṁ tattha । taha vi taē maha trayaṇaṁ kāyavvaṁ savvahā ēkaṁ ॥ 54 ॥
āyaramaggaṁtassa vi niyakhaggaṁ mā hu sē samappējjā । jippihisi na tēṇa tumaṁ khaggasaṇāhō mai sahāē" ॥55
iya jaṁpataṁ mayayaṁ vēttaṇa sasaṁkamāṇasō rāyā । pattō sāhagamūlaṁ nicchiyahiyaō niyayakajjē ॥ 56 ॥
nhaviyatrilittaṁ mayagaṁ maṁḍalagē ṭhāviūṇa tēṇāvi । bhaṇiyaṁ 'niyataravāriṁ appēhi nariṁda ! ēyassa' ॥ 57 ॥
sumariyaḍhaṁravayaṇō rāyā ḍhōyai na tassa asilaṭṭhi । bhaṇai 'bhagavaṁ ! na suhaḍā paharaṇamappiti annassa ॥ 58 ॥
tā ḍhōēhi tumaṁ ciya ahayaṁ ciya tujjha rakkhagō hōhaṁ' । sō bhaṇai 'lōharakkhā naṇu ēsā maṁtasiddhīē ' ॥ 59 ॥
rāyāsse 'ma gharaṁ kuviyakayaṁtō vi pahavaṛa na tumhaṁ । tā kuṇasu kajjasiddhiṁ turiyaṁ mama kaṁdharārūḍhō' ॥60॥
subahu pi bhabhamāṇō jā appara nētra patthivō khaggaṁ । tā ruṭṭhō sō duṭṭhō paiyapuṭṭhō dīhapiṭṭhō vva ॥ 61 ॥
'āyāsiūṇa suiraṁ ēliyamēttaṁ pi kuṇasi na hi vayaṇaṁ' । iya biṁtō saṁbhatō samuṭṭiō kharagavaggakarō ॥ 62 ॥ 15
tō bhaṇitō naravaṇā 'vaha tti lajjāmi tujjha paharaṁtō । ūsarasu diṭṭhimaggā jai pariyāṇāsi appāṇaṁ || 63 ||
dhariūṇa dhammaciṁdhaṁ vaṁcatō dhammiē dhuvaṁ muddhē । dhuttaya ! pattō si na kālamēttiyaṁ kaha ṇu paṁcattaṁ ? ॥ 64 ॥
maha jīviēṇa vēyālasāhaṇaṁ mūḍha ! kāumicchaṁtō । āya-parapunnabhēyaṁ nillakkhaṇa ! kiṁ na lakkhēsi ? ॥65 ॥
10
ēyamāyaniūṇa 'kahamaṇēṇa pariyāṇitō mhi ?' ti satriyakkō liṁgī, 'kukammayārī ya'tti lajjiō, 'niṣphalō
kilēsō 'ti viddāṇō, 'punnapurisō ēsō 'ti galiyapuriyārō, 'kimitō pāvissaṁ ?' ti visannō caiūṇa khaggalaṭṭhi 20
saṁpattapacchāyāvō jōī kayaṁjalī rāyāṇaṁ bhaṇiumāraddhō 'bhō mahānariṁdara । tuha vimalavayaṇakiraṇēhiṁ paṇaṭṭhamiyāṇi
mama maṇōmaṁdirāō mōhatimiraṁ, payaḍībhūyaṁ vivēgaduvāraṁ, uvaladdhaṁ vatthusarūvaṁ, viḍaṁbiō mhi kumittasaṁsaggīē kāla-
mēttiyaṁ, saṁpayaṁ puṇa tumāō kallāṇamittāō parimnāyamuddhamaggō gurumūlapaḍivanapāyacchittō para lōgatthamujjamissaṁ,
kilēsiō ya maē tumaṁ ti khamiyanvō mamāvarāhō, tahā guruparaṁparāgayamatthi mama paharaṇavaṇasaṁrōhaṇaṁ maṇirayaṇaṁ taṁ
mamāṇuragaṇa saṁgōvēu bhavaṁ' ti । rāiṇā vi 'juttamēyaṁ mahābhāga ! tumhārisavivēyiṇō, khamiyavvaṁ ca mamāviṇaya- 25
vayaṇaṁ' ti bhaṇatēṇa 'alaṁghaṇīyatrayaṇō gurujaṇō' ti pucchiūṇa paōgavihiṁ gahiyaṁ maṇirayaṇaṁ ।
ētthaṁtarē vōlīṇappāyā vihāvarī । taō subahuppayāramannōnaṁ khāmiūṇa sa paratthasiddhiuda buddhamāyamāṇasa
gayā dō vi niyaniyadvā ṇēsu । vighnāōdaṁtā vimhiyā maṁtiṇō । pavattiō nayarīē akālē vi mahāmahō । sattarattapajjaṁtē
rattī punacaṁdasurō taō āraṇadēvalōgāō caviūṇa uvavannō guṇamālādēvīē kucchisi puttabhāvēṇa । tayaṇu tāratēya-
maṁḍalaṁ, tihuyaṇatimirabharuddalaṇapaccalaṁ, jiṇanāhassa va pahāmaṁḍalaṁ sūramaṁḍalaṁ ucchaṁgagayaṁ suviṇē pāsiūṇa paḍibuddhā 30

nāṇi vihumāṇaṁ pamōyapulaōlirāhadēhēṇa । namiūṇa kayaṁjaliṇā taō vi paripucchiō ēvaṁ ॥ 184 ॥
'bhayatraṁ ! dayāpahāṇā tubbhē tā maha suyassa ēyassa । rōgōvasamōvāyaṁ kayappasāyaṁ kahaha kē pi ' ॥ 185 ॥

jayai jiṇakapasālō āṇākēṇaīsu jassa līṇēhiṁ । labbhaṁti phalāī supīvarāī ēgaṁtasurasāī || 1 ||
āṇāphalēṇa bhōttūṇa surasuhaṁ sūrasēṇamuṇitiyasō । paḍhamacuō utranō jaṁbuddīvammi bharahammi ॥ 2 ॥
uttaravahē pahāṇē niccaṁ saṁpattaduṣnayapahāṇē | asthi suhiyasajjaṇayaṁ nayaraṁ nāmēṇa gajjaṇayaṁ ॥ 3 ॥
nivaḍiyaganitra''ṇaṁ pi payaḍapaḍipunabahuvihanivāṇaṁ । paravalabhīyaṁ pi sayā adiṭṭhapaḍivakkhasaṁkhōhaṁ ॥ 4 ॥
jattha ya asatthavāhā muiyā dīsaṁti satthavāhā vi । haya-gayasārā vi sayā viyaraṁtā ahayagayasārā ॥ 5 ॥
jattha ya avēyaivivō na baṁbhaṇō sē payaivaggō vi । viṣphurai saṁrasu va sai gharē kamalāmalāmōō || 6॥
jaṁ suhaḍaṁgaṁ va duhā nāṇām̐vaṇarāiyaṁ samaṁtēṇa । suvicittasurāyāraṁ duhā ya taṁ sahai tidivaṁ va ॥ 7 ॥
jassa ya dhavalavisālō gayaṇaṁgaṇalaggatuṁgasiharaggō । rēhai sālō pahuṇō jasō vva saggaṁ pahāviṁtō ॥ 8 ॥
jaṁ ca pāusāyai vva maragaya-tamālanīlēhiṁ dāṇanīradhārāsittamahiyalēhiṁ iōtaōsaṁcaraṁtajalayavigbhamēhiṁ
tuṁgamāyaṁguttamēhiṁ, lalaṁtīhi ya ghōlaṁtakaṇayakuṁḍala-cūḍayapahōvahasiyasōyāmaṇīhiṁ mattakāmiṇīhiṁ, guṁjatēhi ya paṇacci -
yabhatraṇa mayūrēhiṁ maṁgalatūrēhiṁ । sarayāyai vva gōkhīrasacchahāhiṁ samāliṁgiyanahāhiṁ sarayaghaṇāyaṁtīhiṁ pāsāyapaṁtīhiṁ,
kamalāyarāyaṁtēhiṁ ya uddaṁḍapuṁḍarī ēhiṁ nitōviṁtāladdhamagganiccaladviyamahāsāmaṁtataṁtēhiṁ, rāyahaṁsāyaṁtīhiṁ ya dhuvvaṁtadhayavaḍa-

'kiṁ siṁhīsuviggahammi galiyā ēsā mayaṁkassirī ?, kiṁ lacchī kamalāyarassa sayalā pattā'libhīyā ihaṁ ? | 25

bhaṇiyaṁ ca 'bhayavaṁ ! avahatthiyasamattharitthavittharāṇa nissaṁgavaṁbhavvayavarāṇa aṁgīkayavaṇavāsāṇaṁ tumhārisāṇaṁ

'aivala pi aidulla pi aisuṁdaraṁ pi siddhanaṁ । khitrai na kōī kusūlē jāṇaṁtō vatthuparamatthaṁ ॥ 56 ॥

duser kumārō bhaṇiō 'dūrāō āgaō taṁ si । tā kaha kīrau saṁpai vaṁjhō ēsō parikisō ? ॥ 61 ॥

bahupunnapāvaṇijjaṁ rāyasiriṁ pitra paḍiccha tā inhi । bālaṁ bāladivāyaravibuddhasayavattamavanaṁ ॥ 63 ॥

jā jassa sirī nāṇaṁ vināṇaṁ cāga - bhōgasāmaggī । taṁ pāyaḍaṁti ahamahamigāē savvē sunēcchā ।। 90 ॥
tō kayasiṁgārāō maṇibhūsaṇakiraṇajālajaḍilāō । avyaṁgabhōgadēvaṁgasāranēvacchasuhayāō ।। 91 ॥
rahabaramārūḍhāō varamālāvaggavaggupāṇīō । raṁbhā - tilōttamāṇaṁ siṁgārasiriṁ hasatīō ॥ 92 ॥
vimhayatrisaṭṭalōyaṇapaṁkayamālāhiṁ samavimukāhiṁ । rāyataṇaēhiṁ puvtrayaramētra kīraṁtavaraṇāō ॥ 93 ॥
pattāō tāō varakabhayāō līlālasaṁtagattāō । niyaniya kaṁcuidā ijjamāṇamahināhataṇayāō ॥ 94 ॥
pēcchaṁtīṇa ya vivihē kumarē kittijjamāṇaguṇa-gōtē । parisakirīṇa suiraṁ sayaṁvaravaraṁgaṇē ruṁdē ॥ 95 ॥
tammi sumaṇōbhirāmē kumarārāmē samaṁtaō bhamirī । bhamarī va tāsi diṭṭhī lōṇā paumuttarē cētra ।। 96 ॥
khittāō taō tāhiṁ pulayaṁkurahāribāhulaiyāhiṁ । mahu-māilacchīhiṁ va tassa galē kusumamālāō || 97 ॥
tayaṇaṁtaraṁ ca disi disi vaddhāvaṇayaṁ pavajjiyaṁ tūraṁ । ucchaliō ya 'suvariyaṁ suvariya' mii mēlaharō bahalō ||98||
navaraṁ—
10
kaṣnākaḍakkhadhatraliyatrayaṇaṁ paumuttaraṁ palōyaṁtā । jāyā viḍaippajhaṁpiyasasippabhāsssā nivā sēsā ॥ 99 ॥
rayaṇīvirāmatārōhanippahē puhaipālaē daṭuṁ । kuviō kayantaghōrō sāgēyapurāhivō vidurō ॥ 100 ॥
bhaṇai ya 'bhō bhō naranāhanaṁdaṇā ! ajja tumha savvēsiṁ । chinnā imēṇa nāsā dō kamnāō varaṁtēṇa ॥। 101 ।।
tā ginhaha sannāhaṁ saṁpai maṁ pāviūṇa samnnāhaṁ । malimō imassa māṇaṁ pēcchāmō pōrupamāṇaṁ' ॥ 102 ॥
sāmarisā vi saharisā sannaddhā takkhaṇēṇa jamasarisā । patthitra-patthivaputtā vayaṇē vidurassa ujjuttā ॥ 103 ॥ 15
vighnāya tappauttī turiyaṁ caṁdajjhaō vi naranāhō । paumuttaraṁ kumāraṁ allīṇō kayaraṇaggāhō ॥ 104 ॥
bhaṇiō ya viduradraṇa sāmatrayaṇēhiṁ nīiniuṇēhiṁ । 'mā kuṇa samarāraṁbhaṁ caṁdajjhayarāya ! suṇa tattaṁ ॥ 105 ॥
diu imāsimēgā kanā annassa rāyataṇayassa । vijjhāi jēṇa niyamā nivāṇa kōvānalō huliyē ।। 106 ।।
āyārikaṇa savvē dugammi ēgassa dijjamāṇammi । mannaṁti māṇahāṇiṁ dhaiṇiyaṁ narapuṁgavā ēē ॥ 107 ॥
tāiya akīramāṇē niyamā jāmāuyassa bhavaō vi । āruhai tulāē haṁta । jīviyaṁ bahuvirōhēṇa' ॥ 108 ।। 20
taṁ bhai mahuranāhō ' dūyaya ! niuṇō si kūḍamaṁtēsu । pahukajjakaraṇarasiō juttā - 'juttaṁ na bhāvēsi ॥ 109 ॥
dāūṇa sayaṁvaraṇē varaṁ varaṁ kannayāṇa kiṁ kōi । saccapainō naṇu kuṇai annahā sāsasēsō vi ? ॥ 110 ॥
avi ya-
taṁ jaṁpati supurisā taṁ ciya pamuhē kuṇati paḍivati । rayaṇāyarō vva mēraṁ kālēṇa vi jaṁ na laṁghēti ॥ 111 ॥
tā dūya ! bhaṇasu viduraṁ nā'yaṁ nāō kuluggayanivāṇaṁ । jaṁ kannayāṇa kīrai sayaṁvarē variyavaraharaṇaṁ ॥ 112 ॥
na khamaṁ khu akkhamāē karaṇaṁ nāē vi nīisārāṇaṁ । na jaī jayammi jāyai jāu narō nāyapaḍikūlō' ॥113॥
puṇō dūpaṇa bhaṇiyaṁ-

ēyassa natthi mōllaṁ tēlōkkammi vi mahāguṇaḍḍhassa । dāliddapīḍiō haṁ tahā vi viyarāmi lakkhēṇa' ।। 155 ।।
rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ 'bhaṇa kērisā uṇa imassa guṇā ?' । khayarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ 'ēgaṁ tātra mahāpamāṇō, bīyaṁ puṇa suṇaya-
majjārāgaṁjiyaparakkamō, taiyaṁ jatthēsō nisiṁ pi vasaī taṁ paēsaṁ dubālasajōyaṇēhiṁ mr̥sagā pariharaṁti, ēē tātra
pāyaḍā, anē vi aṁtaraṁgā bahavē ēyassa guṇā, tā daṁsēu dēvō ēyaṁ viusavippāṇaṁ, kāravēu mōllaṁ, 'jēṇēyaṁ
vikiṇēmi' ti । taō rāyāēsēṇa nirūvayaṁtēhiṁ diṭṭhō baṁbhaṇēhiṁ tassa uṁduradarakha ō vāmakannō । 'kimērisō

'mama bīyasarīrabhūō tumaṁ, aō jassa pahū tumaṁ tassāhaṁ pahū cētra, tahā dhammabōhisaṁpāyaṇēṇa caiva dinaṁ mama dāyavvaṁ
tumaē, kimanamiō vi suṁdarayaraṁ ? ti ।
tamhā avippauttā pālēmō tāva dō vi rajjāī । rajjōrubhāradharaṇammi pacalā huṁti jā taṇayā ।। 215 ॥
dāūṇa tēsi rajjaṁ kayariṇamōkkhaṁ taō avigvēṇa । sāmannamasāmanaṁ sivasuharasiyā carissāmō' ॥ 216 ॥
harivēgō vi vayāsī 'ēvamiṇa natthi saṁsaō kōī । jaṁ maha maṇē nividdhaṁ tumaē vi tayaṁ phuḍaṁ siddhaṁ ॥ 217 ॥
iya nēhani bharā tē saṁviggā samayakhēttatitthayarē । vaṁdēti pahaṭṭamaṇā nahagamaṇā rāyahaṁsa vtra ।। 298 ॥
sāsayajiṇabhavaṇēsu vikariṁti jattāō aimahantāō। vimhayajaṇaṇīō surāsurāṇa rōmaṁcaciṁcaṁiyā ॥ 219 ॥
pāliti ya dō vikamāgayāī rajjāī jaṇiyacōjjāī । palhāyaṁtā payaīkumudavaṇaṁ jamalacaṁda vva ॥ 220 ॥
paḍaṇī vāraṇāō pūyā - sakāra- viṇayavittīhiṁ । cēiya- muṇīṇa paramaṁ pabhāvaṇaṁ tē karēsī ya ।। 221 ॥
uskā kara bharavajjiyā kayā sāvayā savittaḍḍā । abhuddhariyā iyarē airittavivittadhaṇadāṇā || 222 ॥
sēsāṇaṁ pi jaṇāṇaṁ puvvapattō vi karabharō savvō । taha tēhiṁ taṇuiō jaha jaṇāṇa jāō mahāṇaṁdō || 223॥
uṭṭhantaparyaṁta khalaṁtasuttanī sēsava hujaṇasamūhā । dhannāusadāṇakkhaṇiyajaṁpaṇā tattha saṁvr̥ttā ॥ 224 ॥
laggā jididhammē pāyaṁ baṁbhaṇagaṇā jaṇavayā vi । āsannavōhilāmā anē vi amaccharā jāyā ।। 225 ।।
iya jaṇaṇiyāṇaṁda dhāritā rajjabharadhuraṁ dhīrā । dhavala va tē kayāī gajjayaṁ dō vi saṁpattā ।। 226 ॥
jāyaṁ ca tayāgamaṇē nayaraṁ kayacaḍuladhayavaḍāḍōvaṁ । kiṁkiṇiravakayagīyaṁ payaṭṭana va harisēṇaṁ ।। 227 ॥
kayahāsaṁ va samaṁtā tāḍiyapaḍapaḍahapayaḍapāḍēhiṁ । kayajayajayasadaṁ pitra gaṁbhīramuiṁgara siēhiṁ ।। 228 ॥
tōraṇanibaddhasurataruvaṁdaṇamālāhiṁ gham̐gasamiddhāhiṁ । āiddhanīlamaṇibhūsaṇaṁ va pahudaṁsaṇasayandaṁ ।। 229 ॥
pahuāgamapaimayamayā viyaijjhanaccaṁ tataruṇaramaṇīhiṁ । amarāvai vva rammaṁ taṁ jāyaṁ savvaō nayaraṁ ॥ 230 ॥
pāraddhāō jugavaṁ mahimāō jidicēiyagharēsu । saḍḍhēhiṁ bhattibharanibbharēhiṁ harimullasaṁtēhiṁ ॥ 231 |
kāriti vimāi kamēṇa savvērmu savvajattēṇa । pūyā sakāraṁ gīya-vāiyaṁ divvanahaṁ ca ॥ 232 ॥
dināvāriyasattē jiṇanāhamahāmahē iya pattē । jiṇadhammabaddharāō pāyaṁ payaīgaṇō jāō || 233 ॥

anayā dō vipatthivā jiṇabhavaṇāō sabhavaṇaṁ vacaṁtā pēcchaṁti rāyamaggē abhimuhamāgacchaṁtaṁ viraliyajaḍi-
lasirōruhaṁ taṁbōlāruṇāharōhaṁ dhūlidhūsariyasavtrasarīraṁ sēḍiyādhavaliōbhayapāṇitalaṁ kacchōṭṭiyāmēttanivasaṇaṁ kuppara-

jjhagayaṁ gayaṁ va paḍiyārēhiṁ savvaō lē-kaṭṭāiēhiṁ hammaṁtaṁ kaṁci jūiyarapurisaṁ ।
taō karuṇāvaṇṇacittēṇa paramuttarēṇa 'arē ! mamāvi rajjē kimēsa varāō anāhō itra kayatthijjai ?' tti
bhaṇatēṇā''ṇāviō samāsaṇaṁ, pucchiyā kayatthagā 'arē ! kō ēsō ? kimitthamēvaṁ tubbhēhiṁ kayatthijjai ?' |

ti nicchūḍhō jaṇaēṇa kaō jāipaṁtivajjhō, tahā vi na muṁcai jūyavasaṇaṁ, ramai kara caraṇuttimaṁgāṇaṁ । tannimittaṁ
ca kayatthijjēmāṇō jūiyarēhiṁ pañcāgayahiyaēṇa kāriyāṇēgavisisa hō mōiō jaṇapaṇa sattavārē, chaḍḍiō
vāramēgaṁ sahiēṇāvi tahā vi na viramai । 'jiyaghaṇō vilasara phula- taṁbōlāiēhiṁ na muyai kassai varāḍiyaṁ pi' 5

uvaṇēmō sahiyassa" tti । taō aṇukōsarasāirēgāṇugaō 'ahō ! annāṇaviyaṁbhiyaṁ, ahō ! kammapariṇaī, ahō !

'kiṁ nāma sōiyavvaṁ amnāṇaparavvasē vaṇiyakiyavē ? | abassa khaliyapaḍaṇē kō avarāhō varāyassa ? ॥ 234 ॥
tō va jarā amhē jāṇaṁtayā asārataṁ । asuisarūvēsu raī kuṇamāṇā maṇuyabhō ।। 235 ।।
jaha khalu jahannakammaṁ jūyaṁ viusāṇa garahaṇijjaṁ ca । jāṇiyajiṇatrayaṇāṇaṁ taha niyayaṁ visayasam̐gō vi ॥ 236 ॥
hārē khaṇēṇa jiō jūṇa cirajjiyaṁ jahā vihavaṁ । bisayapasattō sattō taha caiva cirajjiyaṁ sukayaṁ ॥ 237 ॥
uvaēsasahassēhiṁ vi viraō na jahēsa jūyavasaṇāō । avamāṇabhāyaṇāō visayasuhāō tahamhē vi || 238 || 15
baha-baṁdhabhāyaṇamimō jaha jūyāō puṇō puṇō jāō । taha amhē paccāmō puṇō puṇō gabbhakuṁbhī ।। 239 ॥
tā savvā na juttaṁ ēttō visayāmisē sattēhiṁ । saṁpai appāṇaṁ duhaparaṁparābhāyaṇaṁ kāuṁ' ।। 240 ॥
tō pabhaṇai harivēgō 'ṭhiyamēvaṁ mama vi māṇasāvāsē । navaraṁ tumammi nēhō vibaṁdhagō ēttha vatthummi ।। 241 ॥
jāyā dōnhaṁ pi suyā rajja bharunvahaṇapañcalā dāṇiṁ । dāūṇa tēsi rajjaṁ pavvajjaṁ tā pavajjāmō' ॥ 242 ॥
iya maṁtirāṇa tēsiṁ siddhaṁ ubarōhiēṇa sahasa tti । 'kusumaramaṇamujjāṇaṁ rayaṇāyaramunivaī pattō ॥ 243 ॥
guṇasāvaragurusīsō sūrō iva tavasirīē diptō । vēttūṇa dhammasāraṁ va nimmiō jō payāvaraṇā' ॥ 244 ॥
ciravirahiō v ihaṁ dahūṁ tisiō v sisiranīrōhaṁ । guru āgamaṇapautti sōuṁ tē harisiyā sahasā || 245॥
bhaḍacaḍayarēṇa mahayā gaṁtuṁ namiuṁ guruṁ saparivāraṁ । rōmaṁcaṁciyakāyā guruvayaṇaṁ sōumāradvā ॥ 246 ॥
sōūṇa bhavasarūvaṁ jīvāṇaṁ baṁdha mōkkhahēuṁ ca । jiṇasāsaṇadullahayaṁ aṇivayaṁ jīviyassāvi ॥ 247 ॥
rosesōkkhaṁ mukhaṁ muṇicariyaṁ tassa sāhaṇōvāyaṁ । saṁvēgabhāviyamaṇā bhaṇati tē muṇivaraṁ namiuṁ ॥ 248 ॥ 25
'bhayavaṁ ! bhabaṁdhakūvē nivaḍaṁtāṇaṁ apattatāṇāṇaṁ । kuṇasuddharaṇaṁ ahaṁ dikkhāhatthāvalaṁtrēṇa ।। 249 ।।
bhavatuṁgatarubbaddhē dīṇē mōēhi ṇē dayārasiya ! । vayapaharaṇēṇa gihavāsapāsayaṁ dutti chēt ॥ 250 ॥
rāgāivēriyagaṇēṇa hammamāṇāṇamappathāmāṇaṁ । sāmiya! kuṇa sāhijjaṁ saṁpai sēvāpavabhāṇa' || 251 ॥
iya tē bhayasaṁbhaṁtē jaṁpatē muṇivaī samullavai । 'naṇu ēyanimittaṁ ciya gurūhiṁ saṁpēsiō ahayaṁ ॥ 252 ॥
mā kuha kālaharaṇaṁ, turiyaṁ saṁsārasattūbhayaharaṇaṁ । paḍivajjaha saccaraṇaṁ jai maggaha sugarasaṁcaraṇaṁ ॥ 253 ॥
iya guruṇā saṁlattā khaṇēṇa niyaniyapurēsu tē pattā । naṁdaṇavidinnarajjā jāyā dikkhāgahaṇasajjā ॥ 254 ॥
aṭṭhāhiyā sulaṭṭhā kārāviya jiṇaharēsu supaṭṭā | dināvāriyasattā vihiṇā guruaṁtiyaṁ pattā ॥ 255 ॥

puhavīcaṁdacariē sattamē paumuttara- harivēgabhavē dōnhaṁ pavvajjāgahaṇaṁ dēvalōgagamaṇaṁ ca । [ 7. 256-59 ]
pavvāviyā ya vihiṇā rayaṇāyarasūriṇā suguṇanihiṇā । āsēvaṁti sukiriyaṁ anigūhiṁtā niyayatririyaṁ ॥ 256॥
avi ya-
nāṇaṁ ēkkārasaṁgaṁ tava - viyarayā'hijjiyā nijjiyakkhā, sammattaṁ nimmamattā kumayamayaharaṁ nikalaṁkaṁ ghērintā ।
cāritaṁ cārucittaṁ suvihiyavihiṇā duddharaṁ uccahantā, jāyā dihaṁtabhūyā maharisicariē dō vi tē dhīracittā ॥ 257
tavēhiṁ tivvēhiṁ visōsiyaṁgā, mōttūṇa kālē vihiṇā sarīraṁ ।
jāyā taō tē ahamiṁdadēvā, gēvējjagē majjhimamajjhimapi ॥ 258 ॥
tērsi agāhē suhasāgarammi, buḍḍāṇa pamhuḍaduhāṇa bāḍhaṁ ।
anajamāṇā sahasā nisi vva, aicchiyā sāgara sattāvīsā ।। 259 ॥

asthi navīṇaghaṇaghaṇakālavaṇē lavaṇanīranāhē vva । puṁḍavisayammi viulaṁ puṁḍauraṁ aṁtarīcaṁ va ॥ 1 ॥
bahuvihavā naravaṁsā gayakalahā laddhaviddhiṇōṁ jattha | viṁjhammitra bhamaīṁ sayā suhamēva diyāirichōlī ॥ 2 ॥
jattha jaṇō vatthaṁ ci vasaṇaṁ, ayamēva muṇai lōhaṁ ti । aliyaṁ nirlōḍamēva hi, daraṁ tu dhūṇākara khāyaṁ ॥ 3 ॥ 5
kiṁ bahuṇā ?
ārāmaniraṁtarapattaparigayaṁ sālakēsaraṁ sahai । taṁ nayaraṁ mahigayakhuḍiyanālasuvisakamalaṁ va ॥ 4 ॥
tammi bahuvisayasārē kamalōdayasuṁdarē sayāṇiṭṭē । māṇasasarē va haṁsō līlāyai sibilō rāyā ॥ 5 ॥
sabalō visuddha nō, sārō ucchannavērivaggō vi । piyamāyaṁgō va visihasaṁgabaddhaggahō dhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 6॥

piyapēmmāmaya pīṇiyamaṇāṇa saṁpattasavvakāmāṇaṁ । vaccai suhēṇa kālō tāsiṁ saggaṁgaṇāṇaṁ va ॥ 11 ॥ -

[ 8. 13-
samāuttaṁ puttaṁ । suviṇāṇuruvanivvattiyarayaṇasāranāmō vaḍhiō ēsō vi । taō tē dō vi kumāragā nibiḍanēhara-
jjusaṁjamiyā saṁghāḍiyavasaha vva anōnnāvirahēṇa viharanti । kahaṁ ? -
bhuṁjaṁti ramaṁti suvanti jaṁti cidvaṁti dō vi ēgattha । na lahaṁti khaṇaṁ pi raī viōiyā nēllaēṇāvi ॥ 13 ॥
tēsiṁ nēhāisayaṁ pēcchaṁtā dō vi rāya-juvarāyā । niyanēhavilasiyaṁ sumariūṇa lajjōṇayā hunti ॥ 14 ॥
anami diṇē atthāṇasaṁṭhiō siribalō mahārāō । paurēhiṁ pauradukkhāurēhiṁ sahasati vibhattō ॥

'dēva ! tumammi dharantē nimmalajasapasaradhavaliyadharantē । pattā mō guruvasaṇaṁ maggāmō kattha saṁvasaṇaṁ ? ॥ 16 ॥

na khaṇai khattaṁ, dāraṁ na pēllaē, nēya dīsaē kōi । subbai karuṇapalāvī bailāvahīraṁtataruṇīṇaṁ ॥ 18 ॥

'rē rē ! suvasi visatthō vasavattī paṇaiṇīṇa taṁ nūṇaṁ । na bhamasi nayarē ratiṁ muddā vibhuṁjēsi mama vittiṁ ॥ 20 ॥

ginhai thaviyaṁ pi surakkhiyaṁ pi maṇi-kaṁcaṇaṁ kalattaṁ pi । najjaṛa na caiva pāvō iṁtō jaṁtō kayantō vva ॥ 25 ॥

dūrāgaō iva lakkhīyasi jamēyaṁ pucchasi, tā suṇāhi kāraṇamēttha - cōraniggahaṇatthaṁ niggaō na paḍiyāgaō rāya-
siribalanaṁdaṇō girisuṁdarakumārō, tannimittaṁ ca sōyamahanavanivaḍiyassa rāyāilōyassa kicchēṇāicchiō māsō,

dēsiyā nivaes, maggai ṇēgāsu sattasālāsu । gāmaparisāsu pucchara, annēsu vi āsamāīsu ॥ 54 ॥

allīṇō ya kayāī rayaṇīgamaṇāya gāmadēvaulaṁ । vivihadēsāgayāṇaṁ nisuṇai pahiyāṇamullāvē ॥ 56 ॥
jahadivisidvacchērayāī sāhitayāṇa annōnaṁ । ēgēṇa tattha bhaṇiyaṁ bhō bhō ! kiṁ ālajālēhiṁ ? ॥ 57 ॥

15 liyapuriyārō pattō tamanēsiuṁ । suṇai ya ēgattha vaṇasaṇḍē karuṇaṁ ruiyasadaṁ, 'itthiyā varāī kāi' tti samuppanna-

'nisuṇaṁtu lōgapālā !, suṇaṁtu vaṇadēvayāō ! savvāō ! | nīṇēmi hiyayasallaṁ saṁpai tumhāṇa pañcakhaṁ ॥ 151 ॥

balaṁ sasajjhasāē saṁṭhaviyamuttarijjaṁ, bhaṇiyaṁ cāvattaṁ 'tilōyasāhāraṇamiṇaṁ maraṇaṁ pi mē maṁdabhaggāē mudulahaṁ saṁvr̥ttaṁ' |
tāhē samāsāsiūṇa saṁlattā sibilēṇa 'muddhē ! kā tumaṁ ? kiṁ vā tē nivvēyakāraṇaṁ ? jamēvamāyaghāyaṁ vavasiyā si" ।

ēvaṁ ca visaṭṭāmōyavimalakamalālaṁkiē aṇiṭṭiyaviyaḍḍhamahōdaē rajjamahāsarē'bhiramamāṇāṇa tēsiṁ rāyahaṁsāṇaṁ 10

. nisannamattāṇaṁ daṭṭhūṇa suviṇē paḍibuddhō bahalakāgalīgīya saṁvaliyamaṁgala tūranigghōsēṇa girisuṁdaranariṁdō । vimhiō

kayadō saṁtamahōdaya ! dasadisivitthariyanimmalapayāvaṁ । unnaimapattapuvvaṁ gōvara ! pāvēhi sayarāhaṁ ' ॥ 190 ॥
taō 'suviṇatthasaṁvāī pāḍhō 'ti suyaraṁ paṭṭamāṇasō māṇasucchaṁgāō rāyahaṁsō vva samuṭṭhiō sayaṇijjāō ।

maṇimayathaṁbha'bhirāmaṁ rāmāpaḍibimbajōḍakayasōhaṁ । sōhaṁtakaṁtakōṭṭimasaṁkaṁtu llō yamaṇitāraṁ ॥। 192 ॥
tāratavaṇijjanimmiyaduvārasāhāmraṇāliyāruraṁ । ruirasurāgamaraṁjiyavaṁdaṇa - pūyakkhaṇiyabhaviyaṁ । 193 ॥
tattha ya jahāvihāṇaṁ pūyaṁ kāūṇa tihuyaṇapahūṇaṁ । rōmaṁcaciyakāō kayaṁjalī kuṇai thuimēvaṁ ॥ 194 ॥
'nimmalamaūhajālā jayai jiniṁdassa pāyanahapaṁtī | chajjantī nayasuravaimauḍukkhuḍiya vtra maṇisēṇī ॥ 195 ॥

uddāmadāṇajalabudvitutanhālupaṇaibappīhō । ūsiyavicittachattayaṭiviḍikkiyaviyaḍabhūvīḍhō ॥ 78 ॥

'jaya tihuyaṇa bhuvaṇujjōyadīva ! dēviṁdabiṁdakayasēva ! | bhavabhīyajīyasāsaya ! sāsayahadāṇadullaliya ! ॥ 88 ॥

tā paḍikamāhi sammaṁ suṁdara ! dubbhāsiyassa ēyassa । jai kira nēcchasi bhamiuṁ bhīmē saṁsārarannammi" ॥149॥

paḍibhaṇaṛa taṁ kumārō 'kiṁ juttaṁ uttamāṇa piyabaṁdhuṁ । chōḍhūṇa guttibaṁdhē palāyaṇaṁ appaṇā turiyaṁ ? ॥ 226 ॥

nāūṇa nicchayaṁ sē rāyā kaṇayajjhaō kaṇayakēuṁ । niyataṇayaṁ ahisiṁcai rajjē turiō caraṇakajjē ॥ 230 ॥

tē dō vi mahāsattā viyasiyavattā samullasiyagattā | gurujaṇaviṇayapavattā mahāmuṇittaṁ lahuṁ pattā || 233 ॥

parinivvatriti gimhumhatāviyaṁ puhaimaṁḍalaṁ mēhā । junhāmaēṇa bhavaṇaṁ tippē nisaggaō caṁdō ॥ 236 ॥
paccuvayāranirīhā mahādumā diti puppha-phalanivahaṁ । payaīē ciya savvassa vacchalō muṇijaṇō hōi ॥ 237 ॥
taha vi savisēsamēsō bhayavaṁ mama vacchalō jaō imiṇā । bālō vi avālō iva puhaivaittē niuttō mhi || 238 || 30
inhi tu bhīmabhavacārayāō mōiumaṇō vva mēṁ ēsō । sāsēi passayaṁ hiyayasaṁsiyaṁ daṁsayaṁtō vva ॥ 239 ॥
mūḍhō ya ahaṁ ahiyaṁ jō piuṇā daṁsiē vi suhamaggē । iṁdiyavisayavasaṭṭō na payaṭṭō ēttiyaṁ kālaṁ ॥ 240 ॥
1 “yuktam” khaṁ1ṭi• khaṁ2ṭi0 ॥ 2 "prēṣaṇīyāḥ " khaṁ2ṭi0 || 3 bhōttā jē0 ॥ 4 mahaddumā jē0 vinā ॥

ka mārisapurisā paḍaṁti hariṇa vva kūḍapāsēsu । dōggainibaṁdhaṇē rajjabaṁdhaṇē mōhadhaṁdhā || 241 ॥
jiṇanāhammi vi nāhē jīvā jīyanti visayavērīhiṁ । na ramaṁti muttimaggē, balavaṁ khalu kammapariṇāmō ॥ 242 ॥
tāki bahuṇā ? saṁpai karēmi ēyassa bhagavaō vayaṇaṁ । kiṁ kucchiēṇa imiṇā bhīmēṇa bhavāṇubandhēṇa ?' ॥243॥
iya ciṁtābhāviyamāṇasēṇa vēraggamaggalaggēṇa । saṁvēgasārapaṇaēṇa rāiṇā muṇiva bhaṇiō ॥ 244 ॥
'jaha āisaṁti guravō nikāraṇaniddhabaṁdhavā buddhā । taṁ taha karēmi nissaṁkamāṇasō āyahiyakāmī || 245 ॥
ma dhāmahaṁ sirōmaṇī jaṁ gurūhiṁ aṇusahō । na kayāi maṁdapunnāṇa maṁdirē paḍa vasuhārā ॥ 246 ॥
nāṇa suppasanā rōga-jarā-maraṇaharaṇapaḍahacchaṁ । viyaraṁti muttisuhayaṁ uvaēsamahōsahaṁ guruṇō || 247 ॥
tā savvā kumāraṁ rajjē ajjēva jāva ṭhāvēmi । ginhāmi sāmi ! niravajjasaṁjamaṁ tāva pāvaharaṁ' ॥ 248 ॥
guruṇā samaṇunāō sammaṁ namiūṇa tassa payapamaṁ । pattō gihaṁ nariṁdō sāṇaṁda naṁdaṇaṁ bhaṇai ।। 249 ।।
'vaccha ! paḍivajja rajjaṁ ahayaṁ ginhāmi ajja pavvajjaṁ । parivajjiyasāvajjaṁ tāyāinisēviyaṁ vaijjaṁ ' ।। 250 ।।
tō bhai varakumārō 'juttamiṇaṁ tāya ! muṇiyatattāṇaṁ । kiṁtu na viṁdāmi raī tuha muhakamalaṁ apēcchaṁtō ॥259॥
rajjēṇa na mē kajjaṁ, na yāvi bhōēhiṁ nēya lōēhiṁ । jaṛa tā pēcchāmi na iṁdusuṁdaraṁ muhu muhu muhaṁ tē ।। 252 ॥
anaṁ ca na juttaṁ ciya uttamasattāṇa vallahāvacaṁ । muttaṁ mōcūṇa palittamaṁdirē nāsiuṁ turiyaṁ ।। 253 ।।
bhīmama bhavāranē tāyaya ! mayalīvakītramaidīṇaṁ । duhr̥dayataviō vi tumaṁ maṁ mōtuṁ mā palāyāhi' ।। 254 ॥
bhai puṇō naranāhō 'puttaya ! daṁtiṁdiyāṇa pāēṇa । pariṇayatrayāṇa jujjara nippaccūhō samaṇabhāvō || 255 ॥
puṇa bālasahāvō patraddhayadhayasucaṁcalaṁ cittaṁ । na niraṁbhiuṁ samatyō ajja vi tā kēha ṇu pavtrayasi ? || 256॥
ajja vi rajjavilāsā na kayā, na ya māṇiyā samarakēlī । sēcchāvihārasāraṁ na yāṇubhūyaṁ pahutaṁ pi ॥ 257 ॥
uvaladdhavisayatattō pūriyanīsēsakōugō baccha ! । pacchimavayammi niyayaṁ jiiṁdiō pavvajjāsi' ।। 258 ॥
iya bhaṇiō naravaṇā jaṇaṇīē mitta-maṁtiṣamuhēhiṁ । jaṇayasiṇēhā na muyai pavvajjānicchayaṁ kumarō ॥259॥
bhai ya 'taraṁti maṁdā vi tāruyā pōḍhatāruyasahāyā । jujjhati saṁgarē bhīruyā vi sūrassa nissāē || 260 ॥
tāyammi satthavāhē tārunnārannamēyamaiduggaṁ । laṁvējja suddēṇāhaṁ kināma na nicchiucchāhō ? || 261 ॥
dintē hatthālambaṁ tāē acaṁtavacchalē sammaṁ । tuṁgaṁ pi sīlasēlaṁ līlāē āruhissāmi || 262 ॥
tā hīrai hiyayaṁ nitrasirīē dārēhiṁ bhōgasārēhiṁ । purisassa jā na chūṭaṁ pōḍhē saṁtōsapāyārē ॥। 263 ।।
tā viyara sacchaṁdō calō maṇamakkaḍō maṇussassa । jā nāṇasaṁkalāē niviḍīsa nētra saṁjamiō' ॥ 264 ॥
ēvamētanicchiyamaṇaṁ kumāraṁ nāūṇa 'ahō ! dhannō lahukammō mahāsattō ēsō' tti ciṁtayaṁtō dāūṇa
dēvasēṇakumārassa rajja, kusuma kē upamuhapaṁcahiṁ purisasa ēhiṁ battīsāē dēvīhiṁ sunhāhi ya saddhiṁ kayacēiya saṁghasakkārō davā-
viyābāriyasattō saṁpūriyasayala maiggaṇajaṇamaṇōrahō purisasahassa vāhiṇīē sibiyāē mahayā haya-gaya-raha- jōhasāhaṇā-
jugaēṇa dēvasēṇarāiṇā'ṇugammamāṇō gaṁbhīratūranigghōsavahiriya'mbarō amaṁdāṇaṁdabiṁdusaṁdōhapappuyacchō pattō gurusamīcaṁ
rāyā, utrasaṁpannō sapariyaṇō vihāṇēṇa । guruṇā vi pavtrāviō ciivaṁdaṇāikamēṇa । bhaṇiyaṁ ca-
ciivaṁdaṇa rayaharaṇaṁ aṭṭā sāmāiyassa ussaggō । sāmāiyatiyakaḍḍhaṇa payāhiṇaṁ cētra tikkhuttō ।। 265 ॥
vattē nikkhamaṇamahāmahammi vimhaiyasayalanaranāhē | navanavasaṁvēgamuhārasēṇa saṁsittacittāṇaṁ ॥ 266 ॥
caraṇapariṇāmasāhī navapparūḍhō vi pōḍhimaṁ pattō । taha jaha jāyā chāyā jaṇamaṇanēvvāṇasaṁjaṇaṇī ॥ 267 ॥

jā pattē piyasaṁgamē virahiṇā kēṇāvi nō' pāviyā, sāuvvā vyapattiō samujhyā tērsi maṇōnivvuī ॥ 268 ॥
tō tē suṁdarasūriṇō payakaē phulaṁdhuyattaṁ gayā, sutta - tthōruparāgapīṇiyamaṇā tatthēva baddhaggahā ।

aha bhaṇiyā tē guruṇā 'chiṁdaha bhō ! nēhabaṁdhaṇaṁ ēyaṁ । nīharaha jēṇa bhavacārayāō kēṇāvi akkhaliyā ||271
jiṇavayaṇabhāviyāṇaṁ samataṇa-maṇi sattu - mittacittāṇaṁ । na hi juttaṁ saṁjamiuṁ appāṇaṁ nēhaniyalēhiṁ ।। 272 ।।
nēhēṇa tilā vi sati pīlaṇaṁ, taha mahijjaē dahiyaṁ । mailijjai aṁgaṁ ambaraṁ pi nēhāṇu saṁgēṇa ॥ 273 ॥

annaṁ ca-
kō qassa sayā jaṇaō ? kō vā taṇaō suhī va baṁdhū vā । māyā bhaiṇī bhajjā ghyā sunhā va saṁsārē ? ।।275॥
savvō jaṇaō sancō vi naṁdaṇō baṁdhavō rikai mittō । jāō anaṁtakhuttō saṁsārē ēkamēkkassa ॥ 276 ॥
bhutō chuhāirēgā, nihaō vēri tti maccharavasēṇa । parivāliō ya nēhā sancō savvēṇa sayakhuttō ॥ 277 ॥
namiō gurubuddhīē, bhicō dāsō ti dhaṇiyamāṇattō । būḍhō ya, bāhiō vi ya sayasō savvēṇa savvō vi ॥ 278 ॥ 15
iya parittasahāvē saṁsārē muṇiyadhammatacāṇaṁ । rāgō rōsō vi na hōi saṁgaō saṁgarahiyāṇaṁ ॥ 279 ॥
tō bhai kusumakēū 'bhayavaṁ ! bhavabhāvaṇāparassāvi । pasamai na majjha nēhō, na yāṇimō kāraṇaṁ kiṁ pi' ॥ 280 ॥
kusumāuhō vipaṇa 'ēvamiṇaṁ sāmi ! jaṁ suō vayai । jai natraraṁ guruṇō ciya ēttha viyāṇaṁti paramatthaṁ' ||281 ॥
āha gurū 'cirajāō paijammaṁ pōsiō ya tumbhēhiṁ । duparicaō ya tēṇēsa saṁpayaṁ tavarayāṇaṁ pi ॥ 282 ॥
ēyāṇubhāvaō ciya jahuttajiṇadhammakārayāṇaṁ pi । na hi saṁvr̥ttā muttī aviōōgāsaṁsaō tumha' ॥ 283 ॥
kahiūṇa puvvacariyaṁ nīsēsaṁ ōhiṇā parinnāyaṁ । saṁjāyajāisaraṇā puṇō vi guruṇā samaṇusaṭṭā || 284 ॥
tāhē saṁvigamaṇā guruvayaṇāō pihaṁpihaṁbhūyā । bhavabhāvabhāvaṇaparā muṇicariyaṁ cariumāraddhā ।। 285 ॥

samakālamukkagōhaṇaniruddhakuhaṇīsu gaṁtumataraṁtō । jāi khalaṁtapaḍatō hāhāravanibharō kōi ।। 295 ।।
pahabhaggasagaḍasaṁghaḍaṇavāvaḍō dharaṇinivaḍiyakaḍillō । na taraṛa gaṁtuṁ mōttuṁ pi duggaō jalaṇalīḍhō vi || 296 ।।
kāuṁ kaḍīē ēga bīyaṁ bāhāē kaḍḍirī bālaṁ । galiyakaḍilluvarillā palāi bhayaninbharā kāi ॥ 297 ॥
ciraniggayā tri annā bālaṁ sariūṇa sayaṇapamhuddhaṁ । pavisa nēhaparaddhā jālāvalikavaliyaṁ nilayaṁ || 298 ।।
ḍajjhatavaṁsadaṁḍayataḍayaḍataṭṭattaḍāravasuīō । ṭhāṇē cciya kaiṁḍichuṭṭā kā vi ṭhiyā ramaṇabharasruḍhiyā ।। 299 ।।
ḍajjhaṁtasavvasārē savvattha samucchalaṁtapukārē । pavalānilasaṁvaliē huyāsaṇē tammi pajjaliē ॥ 300 ॥
sahasā caiva pattiṁ sunnaharaṁ jattha sō ṭhiō bhayavaṁ । kayasajjhāṇapainnō na palāō sō mahābhāō ।। 301 ॥
chinnasamattamamattō daḍhayaramannannabhāvaṇāsattō । sukkajjhāṇapatrattō acaliyacittō mahāsattō ॥ 302 ॥
aviyāṇiyataṇudāhō hiyayanbhaṁtaranihittajiṇanāhō । avigalasaṁvēgarasō mahāyasō dhariyavīrarasō ॥ 303 ॥
jalaṇapalittaṁ gataṁ caiūṇa samāhisaṁgaō bhayavaṁ । uvavannō suhapannō sañvaṭṭamahāvimāṇammi || 304 ॥
dahūṇa taṁ pāē gāmīṇajaṇō visāyamānō । pamhuṭṭhaniyayadukkhō sōiumēvaṁ samāraddhō ॥ 305 ॥
'hā ! duduha jāyaṁ ēsa mahappā samāhikayaniyamō । nikkhāmiō na kēṇai ēyāō sunnahāō || 306 ||
pattō kalaṁkapaṁka ēyāō dukkayāō ghōrāō । ājammaṁ gāmaṁjaṇō ahō ! mahāpātramiha jāyaṁ ॥ 307 ॥
iya sōiūṇa suiraṁ kāūṇa ya tassa uciyakāyavvaṁ । laggō untriggamaṇō gāmīṇajaṇō sakajjēsu ॥ 308 ॥
aha suṁdaramuṇitraiṇō nicchiyamaiṇō visuddha jōgammi । ghaṇaghāikammaghāyā saṁjāyā kēvaluppattī ॥ 309 ॥
vihiyā ya mahāpūyā sannihiyasurēhiṁ vimhayaparēhiṁ । sāvasthipuravarīē sudaṁsaṇē kāṇaṇē rammē ॥ 310 ॥
tattha ya laddhāvasarō pucchara ukkaṁṭhiō kusumakēū । 'viharai katthēyāṇi kusumāuhamuṇitrarō bhayavaṁ 1' ।। 311 ।।
kēvalī sē jahadviyaṁ savvamēva vr̥ttaṁtaṁ । uppatti ca vimāṇē savvaṭṭē niṭṭhiyāṇiṭṭē || 312 ॥
maṇai 'suladdhaṁ jīyaṁ maharisiṇō tassa pūyapāvassa । taha ghōrē uvasaggē jēṇa tahā''rāhiō appā || 313 ||
kīrai saṁgañcāō, suhēṇa tapijjaī tavaṁ ghōraṁ । vihurāvaḍiyāṇa jayammi dullahā''rāhaṇapaḍāyā ॥ 314 ॥
taṁ yējjaṁ taṁ ghējjaṁ sā lēsā sō parakkamō vimalō । tārisaē uvasaggē jāyai tassēva dhannassa ।। 315 ॥
tamhā na sōiyanvō sa mahābhāgō tara samaṇasīha ! । milihisi asaṁsayaṁ ciya tumaṁ pi sē yēvakārēṇa || 316॥
daliyamiva kammasēnaṁ, tinnō vtra bhavōdahī bhavaṁtēhiṁ । tā mā kāsi mahāyasa ! adhiī yēvaṁ pi hiyayammi' ॥317॥
kēvaliṇā''ṇattō saṁviggō kusumakēumuṇivasabhō । savisēsaṁ saṁsārāsārataṁ ciṁtiuṁ suiraṁ ।। 318 ॥
vērammāisayāō'ṇunāō sūriṇā samāraddhō । suttabhaṇiēṇa vihiṇā sammaṁ saṁlēhaṇaṁ kāuṁ ।। 319 ।।
kāsī ya vicittatavaṁ caurō saṁvaccharē suicaritō । vigaīvivajjiyāī puṇō vi cattāri vāsāī ॥ 320 ॥
ēgatarōvavāsō dō vāsē ambilēṇa pāriyavaṁ । aviṭṭitavaṁ kāsī chammā sē parimiyā''yāmaṁ ॥ 321 ॥
chammāsē u vigiddhaṁ tavaṁ tavēsī tamēva pāraṇayaṁ । saṁvaccharaṁ tu ēkaṁ kāsī ya niraṁtarā''yāmaṁ ।। 322 ॥
parisrusiyapisiya-ruhirō camma- dvi-nasāvasēsataṇulaṭṭhī । gurupayamūlē sammaṁ salluddharaṇaṁ taō kāsī ॥ 323 ॥
āhārapariccāyaṁ kāūṇa gurūṇamaṇumaō sammaṁ । girikaṁdarammi rammē pāyavagamaṇaṁ aha patrabhō ।। 324 ॥

saṁmuddhaṁ suddhalēsaṁ gaya-bhayarahiyaṁ rūvasuṁdērasīmā, taṁ sapattā pavittaṁ sucariyacaraṇā dō vi tē dhammadēvā || 327॥

[ ēgārasamō puhavīcaṁda guṇasāyarabhavō ]
10
jayai jiṇavayaṇagaṁbhīrasāyarō jattha sīlarayaṇāī । lahiūṇa sukayamukayā jaṁti paraṁ nivvuī dhīrā ॥ 1 ॥
asthi suvisaggāmō bahukaṇayālaṁkiō ghaṇavaṇō ya । saṁpannavahupasāō suhaḍō iva bharahanupasiddhō || 2 ॥
sunvaṁtaviulaghōsō phaliō v mahādumō sunaikaliō । pahiyasamatāvanāsō ramaṇīō kōsailō dēsō ॥ 3 ॥
puṁḍucchuvāḍavaha māṇajaṁtacuṁkāramuhaladisiyakō । sughaṇasahayārakāṇaṇaviṇivāriyamihirakarapasarō ॥ 4 ॥
sāmōyakalamagōvīsaṁgīyayasavaṇakhaliyagamaṇēhiṁ । paihiēhiṁ maēhiṁ ya niccalēhiṁ cacikiusō ॥ 5 ॥
sayalasirīṇa nivāsē dēsē ēyammi atthi supayāsā । bahupayaipūriyāsā purī ajha ti nāmēṇa ॥ 6 ॥
dō visamāsu jīsē paḍhamajiniṁdassa rajjakajjēṇa । kīrai cārunivēsō surēhiṁ surarāyatrayaṇēṇa ॥ 7 ॥
chajjai paisaṁḍighaḍiō maṇikiraṇābaddhasakakōdaṇḍō । pāyārō parivēsō vba bhāṇuṇō mahiyalāvaḍiō ॥ 8 ॥
bhavaṇēhiṁ rayaṇa-maṇinimmiēhiṁ sayayaṁ payaṭṭanahiṁ । bhōgubbhaḍalōēhi ya jā suranayariṁ visēsēi ॥ 9 ॥
jattha viyaraṁtavilayāmaṇikuṁḍala kaṁtidaliyatimirēsu । udaya-'tthaimaṇaṁ raviṇō na muṇijjai jāu bhavaṇēsu ॥ 10 ॥
sairalā supattaphalayā jattha bhaḍā pāyavā vi sacchāyā । nārsēti saṁsiyāṇaṁ paratāvaṁ samaṁtēṇa ॥ 11 ॥
jattha panavilayāsarīrāṇīva viḍaṁkasaṁsiyāī, kuṭṭaṇīhiyayāṇīva mahālōhaggalāī, mahāsarāṇīva kamalōdayā-
15 virahiyāī, supurisahiyayāṇīva suvisālāī, saṁsāṁracariyāṇi va vicittacittasārāī maṁdirāī । tahā muṇiṇō vva
suhāsā, haṁsā iva visuddhōbhayapakkhā, kariṇō vtra pasaratasammayā, mayāriṇō vtra sukēsarā jaṇavisarā । tahā sajjaṇā
iva bahulā, jiṇabhattā iva sudhanapubhā, taruṇabhāvā iva payāsiyamuttāhalujjalarayaṇā, vēsāvilāsā iva dāviya-
bahuvihanē ttaviyārā, sukaikavvabaṁdhā iva sutrannayapasāhiyā, jiṇā iva dāviyābhayā, kēsavā iva sāmalayā, thērī iva

kanakēna, bahubhiśca kaṇaiḥ kaiśca - jalairalaṅkr̥taḥ । ghanāni vraṇāni vanāni ca yatra । sampannaḥ prabhuprasādō yasya, sampannāni bahūni prakr̥ṣṭāni ca śākāni
yatra । [ gā0 3 - ] śrūyamāṇō vīnāṁ kulasya ghōṣō yatra, śrūyamāṇāśca vipulā ghōṣāḥ - gōkulāni yatra । suṣṭhu natyādibhi ( natibhiḥ nadībhi )va
kalitaḥ । pathikānāṁ śramaṁ tāpaṁ ca nāśayati" ॥ 2 kōsalādēsō jē0 vinā ॥ 3 pahipahi ya mahipachi ya ni bhrā0 ॥ 4 saṅkētaḥ-
"pasaṁḍiti suvarṇam" ।। 5 svarṇa 2 bhrā0 ॥ 6 saṁkēta:- " śarān lānti- gr̥hṇantīti śaralāḥ [ saralāśca ] । suṣṭhu prāptaṁ
phalakaṁ - khēṭakō yaiḥ, śōbhanāni patrāṇi phalāni ca yēṣu । sacchāyāḥ - saśrīkāḥ sātapābhāvāśca । parēbhyaḥ santāpaṁ prakr̥ṣṭasantāpaṁ ca " ॥ 7
saṁkēta:- "[ viḍaṁkētyādau, ] viṭānāmaṅkē saṁśritāni, viśva- varaṇḍikābhiḥ śaṁsitāni ślāghitāni । mahatā lōmēna argalāni adhikāni,
mahatī ca lōhārgalā yēṣu । kamalānvitairudakaiḥ kamalōdayēna cāvirahitāni । suṣṭhu viśālāni, suṣṭhu viśiṣṭāśca śālā yēṣu । citrāṇi -
āścaryāṇi ālēkhyāni ca ॥ 8 saṁsārica' jē0 vinā ॥ 9 saṅkēta:- " [ suhāsayētyādau, ] śubhāśayāḥ suhāsyakāśca । prasaran sammadaḥ
sammataṁ ca yēṣām । saṣṭhu kēsarāṇi yēṣām śōbhanasya ca kasya sukhasyēśvarāḥ " ॥ 10 saṅkēta:- " [ nēhētyādau,] snēhaḥ- prēma ghr̥tādi
ca । suṣṭhu dhanyāḥ puṇyāśca sudhānyēna ca pūrṇāḥ । radanāḥ- dantāḥ ratnāni ca vajrādīni । nētrāṇi cakṣūṁṣi tēṣāṁ vikārāḥ, vastraviśēṣādha
tēṣāṁ vikārāḥ । suvarṇakāḥ- dēśādivarṇanāni, suvarṇakaṁ ca- kanakam dāpitābhayāḥ, darśitā abhayāḥ- harītakyō yēṣu । śyāmalakāḥ sāmala-
kāśca । śōbhanam akṣasūtraṁ yajñōpavītam, akṣāṇāṁ ca - bibhītakānāṁ sūtra-sūtraṇā yēṣu । mahad garē - viṣam, mahaca agaru - gandhadravyam ।
surasēnayā, suṣṭhu rasēna - pāradādinā, anugatāḥ । suṣṭhu vēśyānāṁ vārakā yēṣām, vaiśa (vēsa ) vāraśca - pratītaḥ । nāgarājēna, nāgarasya ca - suṇṭhayā
āyēna - lāmēna, sārā । nānāmārgā, nāṇāvaṭṭaśca - prasiddhaḥ " ।। 11 " brāhmaṇāḥ " khaṁ2ṭi0 ॥

।
tīē ya sōhaggāisayatuliyāmōyarō paṇa paṇaiṇīviṁdā maṁda mōyarī pañcahavūhōbagīyamāṇaparakkamō alaṁghiya-

jaṇaō jaṇassa, dhaṇaō dhaṇatthiṇaṁ, kucariyāṇa kīṇāsō । mārō daiyāṇa, susēvayāṇa cintāmaṇī ēsō ॥ 15 ॥
saraṇāgayāṇa basaṇē, sayaṇē daiyāṇa, saṁgarē'rīṇaṁ । dāṇavvasaṇī va vaṇaṁ puṭṭhi na kayāi sō dēi ॥ 16 ॥
cittaṁ jaṁ tassa jasō sasaṁka -kuṁdujjalaṁ pi aṇavarayaṁ । gāyaṁtīṇa vi kasiṇaṁ karēi vayaṇaṁ riuvahūṇaṁ ॥ 17 ॥
amnaṁ pi mahācittaṁ uttamarāō vi jaṁ imō niccaṁ । duriyamērāē mēhaṇīē uccahai nādattaṁ ॥ 18 ॥
tassa ya suvittamōttiyaguṇāsayā vihiyahiyayasuhasōhā । suvisuddhasamāyārā maṇōharā hāralaiya vva ॥ 19 ॥
antēurappahāṇā dēvī dēvi vva sai suhāhārā । nayaṇavilāsōhāmiyapaumā paumāvaī nāma ॥ 20 ॥

jāēṇa vāsabhavaṇaṁ pabhāsiyaṁ nahayalaṁ va caṁdēṇaṁ । puhaīvaī ya hōhī ēsō tā puhaicaṁdō ti ॥ 29 ॥
aha paṁcadhāikarakamalalāliō jāisaraṇasaṁbuddhō । kayajaṇayasammaō sammaō ya navajōvaṇaṁ pattō ॥ 30 ॥
navaraṁ na kuṇai kēliṁ, na ya dūmai kaṁ pi pharusavayaṇēhiṁ । na hasai, na caiva vilasai suparāṁtō vīyarāgō vva ॥31॥
bāhara na gaya-turaṁgē, na ya paharaṇaguṇavaṇē kuṇai kōḍuṁ । mallā 'laṁkārapasāhaṇāṇi babahāra kui || 32 ||
bhattō māi-piūṇaṁ, bhattō jiṇacēiyāṇa sāhūṇaṁ । bhattō jiṇamuṇisēvāparāṇa sāhammiyāṇaṁ pi ॥ 33 ॥
tō ciṁta harisī hō ' kaha nāma imō aṇaṁgasarisaṁgō । bhōgōvabhōgamaggē laggissai rāyasuyajōggē ? ॥ 34 ॥
salahijjara jilōē rāyakumārāṇa jōvaṇāraṁbhē । siṁgārahāri cariyaṁ samujjamō vērivijaē ya || 35 ॥
ēvaṁ vipra jasō savvattō sarayasasaharapayāsō । tēō sirī pahuttaṁ jāyaṛa appaḍihayaṁ ēvaṁ || 36॥
ēsa uṇa muṇiva iva pasaṁtacittō aṇiparapīḍō । hōhī gammō ujjhiyaparakamō dubviṇīyāṇaṁ ॥ 37 ॥
tā pattālamēyaṁ kārēmi kalattasaṁgahaṁ tātraṁ । tavtrasagaō sayaṁ ciya kāhī savvaṁ jaō bhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 38 ॥
tā chēō tā māṇī tā dhammī tāva ujjuō sōmō । jātra gharaṭṭō vva narō na bhāmiō daḍḍhamahilāhiṁ ॥ 39 ॥
kariṇō siṇīhiṁ, vaggāhiṁ vāiṇō, gōsuryāṁ vi natthāhiṁ । kīraṁti vasē purisā marālalīlāhiṁ mahilāhiṁ ॥ 40 ॥

ēyāō vi bahūō mōttūṇa suvallahaṁ sayaṇavaggaṁ । dūrāō āyāō anajjamāṇassa maha kajjē ॥ 54 ॥
iya mōhavinaḍiyajaṇē saṁsārē akkataruphalāsārē । na khamaṁ khaṇaṁ pi ramiuṁ bhāviyatattāṇa sattāṇaṁ ।। 55 ।।
agaru nibbaṁdhō jaṇaṇī-jaṇayāṇa ēttha vatthummi | nēhanaḍiyāī tāī na sarhati khaṇaṁ pi maha virahaṁ ।। 56 ।। 10
ubvāhiyāō dūrāgayāō pēmumbhaḍāō ēyāō । muñcantīō vālāō mōhāō huṁti duhiyāō || 57 ॥
nava jaṇō mōhā niṁdara maṁ pavtrayaṁtamēttāhē । tāyāṇurōhaō hī ! paḍiō kaha saṁkaḍē ahayē ? ॥ 58 ॥

avi ya-
hōi amayāō ahiō navanēhē lajjamāṁṇamihuṇāṇaṁ । pariyaṇamajjhē cōriyanirikkhiē diṭṭhisaṁjōgō ॥ 66 ॥

yāhiṁ 'avitahamēyamajjauttēṇaṁ sāhiyaṁ bhavasarūvaṁ, aha kō uṇa ēyapariharaṇōvāō ?' tti । kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ 'suguru-
vayaṇāō suddhadhammāsēvaṇaṁ, sugurū vi jō imiṇā suvidiyālavigbhamēṇa bhōgasuddēṇa na mōhijjai' ti । tāhiṁ
bhaṇiyaṁ 'ajjautta ! tumamēva paramatthavōhaṇēṇa amha gurū, kayatthībhūyāō vayaṁ tuha ghariṇīsadēṇa, viyaliyā tuha vaya-
20 ṇāō bhōgatanhā, tā karēhi saṁpai sugurusamappaṇēṇa suddhadhammacaraṇasaṁpattimamhāṇaṁ, tumhāṇaṁ pi muṇiyatattāṇaṁ na juttaṁ
muhuttaṁ pi ēttha pamāiuṁ, palittamaṁdirōvēhaṇaṁ khu ēyaṁ, ahavā tumamēva bahuṁ viyāṇāsi' ti । taō 'paḍibuddhāō
ēyāō vitti pamuiēṇa bhaṇiyāō kumārēṇa 'sāhu, suṁdarī bhē vivēgō, na dullahō bhē suddhadhammō, saphalā bhē
maṇuyatta-khētta-kula- rūtravibhāṇāisāmaggī, samāsanā ṭhiyā'sēsa kilē savippauttamuttisaṁpattī, tā ciṭṭhaha tātra paṁcapara-
mēpirititiāō savvasattāṇukaṁpirīō piyabhāsirīō aparōvayāviṇīō jāva samīhiyasāhaṇē'vasaraṁ labhāmō'
25 tti । paḍivanamēyaṁ sannāhiṁ । tappabhi ca dhammaviyārābhirayāṇa vaccamāṇēsu diṇēsu viṭṭhavayaṇāō vināō ēsa
vr̥ttaṁttō rāiṇā, ciṁtiyaṁ ca 'na ēsa mahilāhi vasīkaō, avi mahiliyāō cētra imiṇā virāgīkayāō, tā
niujēmi ēyaṁ rajjadaṁdē, jēṇa tavbāulyāē vīsārēi dhammavattaṁ pi' । tti nicchiūṇa nivēiyaṁ dēvīē । tīē vi
bhaṇiyaṁ 'dēva ! diṭṭhō maē sumiṇaō, kira kumārō tumaē ujjallāē nivēsiō niyasīhāsaṇē, taō sasiṁhāsanō
caiva uppaiūṇa ṭhiō pāsāyasiharē, tayaṇu viṣphuraṁtaphāratēyapavbhārēṇa bhāsiyāsēsabhuvaṇēṇa tēṇa dāūṇa hatthāvalambaṁ
30 ahaṁ tumaṁ cā''rōviyāī tatthēva, paṇamiyāī savvalōēṇaṁ ti, aō suviṇōvalaṁbhāō najjai sōhaṇaṁ saṁpahāriyaṁ dēvēṇa,
bhavissas paramadayabhāyaṇamēvaṁ kumārō' ti ।

sāmatthiūṇa ēvaṁ gōsē payapaṇamaṇatthamaṇupattō | dināsaṇōviṭṭhō bhaṇiō kumarō duvēhiṁ pi ॥ 100 ॥
'dhannō sivaccha ! kayakaya saṁcaō, vallahō si jaṇayāṇaṁ । umbarapasūṇadulahō jīviyasañcassabhūō si ॥ 101 ॥

chajjā, na uṇa mārisō kāburisakasarō ahavā tubbhē cētra pamāṇaṁ, āṇavēha jahājuttaṁ puṁttakiṁkaraṁ' ti । taō 'ahō !
jaṇayavacchalō vigīyaviṇaō ya mē naṁdaṇō' tti bhaṇantēṇa agghāiūṇa matthara gaṇayanirūviē pasatthamuhuttē'bhisittō 15
subaḍavicchaḍḍēṇa rajjē puhaicaṁdō, paṇamiō sayaṁ, tayaṇu sāmaṁtāīhiṁ । 'jaya mahārāō' ti patrattō baṁdidibahala-
mailaharō, pavajjiyāī maṁgalatūrāī, paṇaciō vāravilāsiṇīsaṁdōhō, uvaṇayāī gaya-turaya-raha-paharaṇa rayaṇā-'laṁkārāi-

iya nihuyaṁ jhāyaṁtō sumaraṁtō puvyajammiyaṁ suttaṁ । saṁpāviyasajjhāṇō saṁpattō kēvalannāṇaṁ ॥ 201 ।।

amhē vi unnāō saṁpattō jāhi muttinuharasiō । sōmasahāvō ēsō siddhipurīmaggasatthāhō ॥ 204 ॥
ēyāṇumaggalaggā sammaṁ dhammaṁ sunimmalaṁ cariuṁ । kāhāmō'sēsabhavubbhavāṇa dukkhāṇa vōcchēyaṁ ॥ 205 ॥

āvūriyaṁ ca tavvēlamēna gayaṇaṁgaṇaṁ suragaṇēhiṁ । paḍapaḍahapāḍapaḍi ravamuhaliyapāsāyakōḍēhiṁ ॥ 207 ॥

ghōlaṁtakannakuṇḍalasuramaṇḍalamaṇḍiyaṁgaṇaṁ bhavaṇaṁ । taṁ daṭṭṇa pattō savimhaō purajaṇō ēvaṁ ॥ 209 ॥
'bhō bhō ! pēcchaha cōjjaṁ jamajja vārējjaē vaṇivarassa । punōhasamāiṭṭhā surā vi baddhāvayā pattā ' ।। 210 ॥

219
hā ! kaha jāṇatō ciya paḍiō haṁ rajjakūḍajaṁtammi | gurujaṇadakkhiśnatrasā vasārasā mattadaṁti v ? || 218 ||
hōhī suvāsarō sō kaiyā haṁ jammi dhammiyajaṇammi । aggamaṇīṇa muṇīṇaṁ majjhē gaṇaṇaṁ lahissāmi ? ॥ 219 ॥
kaiyā gurupayapaṇaō nāṇa-carittāṇa bhāyaṇaṁ hōhaṁ ? । kaiyā uvasamalacchī vacchē ramihī mama jahicchaṁ ? ॥ 220 ॥
samasattu - mittacittō susāṇa sumnahara - sēlasiharēsu । ussaggē ṭhāissaṁ kaiyā sajjhāṇathirabhāvō ?' ॥ 221 ॥
susāṇa-sumnahara -
iya ullasantasaṁvēgagururasō'puvtrakaraṇalābhēṇa । sivapayagamanissēṇiṁ va khavagasērṇi samārūḍhō || 222 ॥
siyajhāṇaghaṇēṇa khaṇēṇa tēṇa ghaṇaghāikammasaṁghāyaṁ । saṁcuniūṇa saṁpattamuttamaṁ kēvalambhāṇaṁ ॥ 223 ॥

paḍivanadavvaliṁgassa takkhaṇā puhaicaṁdakēvaliṇō । jayajayaravamuhalasurāhivēṇa vihiyā taō mahimā || 225 ||
kaṇayakamalōyaraṁkē ṭhaviūṇa mahāmuṇi muṇiyatattō । harisiyamaṇō suriṁdō sāṇaṁdō thōumāraddhō ॥ 226 ॥

tūsai payāṇa bahusaṁpayāṇa, dīṇāṇa dēi supayāṇaṁ । lajjai jaṇēṇa parimiyadhaṇēṇa sīyaṁtavimaṇēṇa || 237 ।।

cāraṇagaṇēṇa gijjai sayalāsu sahāsu tassa māhappaṁ । jō ahiō sō paḍhamaṁ savvattha vi lahai sammāṇaṁ ॥ 240 ॥
aha asthi tattha'ṇagvēyabhūrirayaṇēsarō dhaṇayasēṭṭhī । na ya ūsavēi sō ūsavē vi kira vējayantīō ॥ 241 ॥
tassa ya suyā payāmaṁ pasiddhisaddhāluyā agijjaṁtā । mannanti māṇahāṇi samatrayamittāṇa majjhagayā || 242 ॥
tē vighnavinti jaṇayaṁ puṇō puṇō kōḍikēukaraṇatthaṁ । sō bhaṇaī 'nō muṇijjai puttaya ! tumhāṇa dhaṇasaṁkhā ||243 ॥
saṁkhānicchayavirahā na hi juttā kē kappaṇā ēsā । aliyavayaṇaṁ khu ēyaṁ nēvuciyaṁ uttamajaṇassa' ॥ 244 ॥
vāraṁ vāraṁ vinivāriyā va tē vaṇivarēṇa dummēhā । viramaṁti nō varāyā duvvavasāyāō ēyāō || 245 ।।
paḍikūliumasamatthā vayaṇaṁ jaṇayassa sannihigayassa । ciṭṭhati dēsakālaṁ vimaggamāṇā mahabhāṇā ॥ 246 ॥
ammi dinē dhaṇaō nimaṁtiō nidvabaṁdhuṇā dhaṇiyaṁ । katthaī kajjē bhavvē pattō nayaraṁtaraṁ anaṁ ॥ 247 ॥
ladvāvasarēhiṁ taō dhaṇēsarāīhi dhanayataṇaēhiṁ । savvāī rayaṇāī vikkīyāī turaṁtēhiṁ ॥ 248 ॥
gaṇiūṇa dhaṇaṁ tattō vihiyā kōḍijjhayā pamujhaēhiṁ । jāyā, savvajaṇāō aha ahiyā tēsi parisaṁkhā || 249 ॥
tō baṁdividavagnijja māṇakula- cāya- bhōyamāhappā । savvē vi haṭṭatuṭṭā maṁtinti parōparaṁ ēvaṁ ।। 250 ॥
'ancō ! niratthayaṁ pattharēhiṁ gharasaṁṭhiēhiṁ mudrā mō । vuḍḍhattavivaḍhiyadummaissa tāyassa buddhī' ॥ 259॥
tētriya gāhaganigamā rayaṇāī tāī niyaniyapurēsu । annannadisāgayanēgamāṇa viyariṁ savvāī || 252 ।।
dhaṇaō tri gihaṁ pattō puttē pucchara 'kimēyamāyariyaṁ । niyakulalahuttahēū kēuvihāṇaṁ bhavaṁtērhi ?' ।। 253 ॥
tē cci kati savvaṁ jahaṭṭhiyaṁ tuṭṭamāṇasā tassa । rayaṇaviṇiōgavattaṁ niyama vihavaṁ pasaṁsaṁtā || 254 ॥
padaṁti ya-
'kiṁ tīē sirīē supītrarāē channāē gēhaniyāē । tripphurai jaē na jaō miyaṁkakiraṇujjalā kittī ?' || 255
i si āruṭṭō paṇa tē suddha niṭhuraṁ sēṭṭhī । 'dujjammajāyanivbhaggasēharā ! rē mahāmukkhā ! ॥ 256 ॥
savvaṁ pi vittamēyaṁ na hōi mōllaṁ mamēgarayaṇassa । iya hāriūṇa riddhiṁ paṁḍiyavāēṇa kaha bhaggā ? ॥ 257 ॥
tā nissaraha turantā mama gēhāō kubuddhiyā savvē | āṇēha vā turaṁtā savvāī majjha rayaṇāī' ।। 258 ॥
pariyāṇiyaduccariyā piuṇā ninbhacchiyā taō savvē । vaṇināma-dhāma - vibhāṇavirahiyā tē samuccaliyā ।। 259
bhamiyā ya ciraṁ mahimaṁḍalammi viulammi tē vigayabhaggā । na ya savvarayaṇajōyaṁ pattā tē saṁbhavābhāvā ॥ 260॥

sīliṁgā mahāmahaggharayaṇaṁ khaṁtāimuttāsayaṁ, sāmanaṁ sunihiṁ va saṁjamatatrōmāṇikacaccikkiyaṁ ।
